Important News

Inside Story of the Resignation of Komai, the Puppet Chief of Manchuria 丨Nanguang丨 86

Japanese Officials Attacked for Corruption and Misconduct

Policy of Co-opting General Ma Zhanshan Fails

Internal Strife and Conflicting Views Cause Dilemma

Financial Difficulties and Inability to Cope Bring Despair

1. Komai to Request Resignation from Tokyo

Komai Tokusaburo, the Supreme Emperor of the Puppet State of Manchuria and Chief of General Affairs of the Puppet State's State Council, according to a Tokyo telegram yesterday, Komai will arrive in Tokyo soon to submit his resignation to the Japanese Cabinet. It is proposed that Maruyama Tsurukichi succeed him. Komai's resignation was rumored once in mid-June, but was subsequently cancelled after persuasion from puppet dignitaries. However, the Japanese side did not dare to disclose the content. According to our sources, the main reasons are threefold: firstly, the opposition of Japanese officials; secondly, the complexity of financial issues; and thirdly, the strategy to deal with the Volunteer Army. Details are elaborated below in separate sections.

2. Corrupt Japanese Officials Permeate the Northeast

Within the puppet state, there are approximately three types of Japanese officials who are fighting, opposing, and resisting each other: firstly, the opposition between the civilian faction and the military faction; secondly, the opposition between honest officials and corrupt officials; and thirdly, the opposition between the Fascist Party and the Liberal Party. According to statistics, there are more than 150 Japanese officials in the various agencies of the puppet central government of Manchuria. As for the local agencies and the newly seized customs, salt administration, postal service, and the former Chinese state-owned railways, Japanese personnel have also been gradually installed, and the number is increasing daily. It is impossible to know the details accurately. However, Japanese officials, depending on the size of the agency recommended by their background and the strength of their backers, often engage in open and covert struggles, each showing their abilities. In particular, those recommended by the military閥 are the most arrogant. This Northeast Incident has relied on the power of the military in everything, expanding the Japanese situation in the Northeast, thus leading to the opposition between the civilian faction and the military faction. Moreover, the military department believes that the puppet organization of Manchuria should be subordinate to the Governor-General of Kwantung, without the need for further concealment, and should take this opportunity to directly control it as a colony. Civilian officials, on the other hand, argue that they should not immediately abandon their masks, but should outwardly advocate respecting the slogans of the Chinese people in order to reduce international resentment. Therefore, while prioritizing Japanese interests, they dare not treat the Chinese people harshly, and fear that the Chinese people will suddenly change, which will be detrimental to the Japanese. As a result, they will inevitably want to achieve quick success, abandon their name, and take the reality, which is the best policy. However, radical soldiers have always opposed this view. This is the opposition between the civilian and military factions.

Secondly, there is the resistance between corrupt officials and honest officials. Originally, most of the Japanese officials recommended by the Japanese army in the Northeast were ruffians and vagrants used by the Japanese military for many years, that is, the so-called Manchurian ruffians or China experts. It is natural for villains to be successful and do all kinds of evil. Since the September 18th Incident, the Japanese army has commended and cherished their past achievements in disrupting China over the years, and in order to use their so-called China expert skills, they have vigorously recommended them to the puppet state, assigning them to important official positions. These people are morally corrupt and inherently greedy. In the past, they relied on the power of their country in China to sell drugs and harm the country, relying on their power to bully others. They are also accustomed to a life of debauchery. In addition to knowing a little about the situation in China and secretly reporting to their country, they have no skills to deal with the world. It is said that since the puppet state came to power, the consumption of the Japanese tavern Yachiyo in Changchun (that is, a tavern兼堂子) has been statistically over tens of thousands of yuan a night, all spent by the puppet state's Japanese officials indulging in prostitution. Moreover, after the Japanese officials came to power, Japanese taverns in various places were full. This can be used as ironclad evidence of the Japanese officials' corruption and debauchery and exploitation of the people's wealth. This is still not enough to fully describe the corruption of the puppet state's Japanese officials. Now, let's give an account of the extortion of a few prominent officials to inform the people of the country. For example, Horii, the Japanese adviser to the Harbin Shipbuilding Bureau, has extorted tens of thousands of yuan in less than three months since taking office. Xie Jieshi, the puppet foreign minister, has also reached more than one million yuan in less than three months. Xie Lyuxi, the representative of Rehe, has also pocketed more than 120,000 yuan in less than a month. These are the most obvious examples. This kind of corruption is mostly sheltered by Komai, the Chief of General Affairs, or caused by insufficient supervision. Officials who are a little more disciplined are afraid of being implicated and suspected, and are very dissatisfied with their behavior. There are many who secretly criticize them, so there is another opposition. This is the content that Tokyo has long wanted to persuade him to resign.

3. Failure to Co-opt Ma Zhanshan

Four Puppet Officials Act as Guarantors

In addition to what was described above, Komai's resignation is due to the failure to take responsibility for the policy of co-opting General Ma Zhanshan. The Japanese military閥 has always advocated resolving Ma Zhanshan by force, but the civilian officials represented by Komai advocated co-opting General Ma through a bribery policy, saying that otherwise the Japanese army would suffer heavy casualties. The military department reluctantly agreed and sent Xie Jieshi to meet with General Ma. After several consultations, General Ma, in order to endure humiliation and achieve great success, feigned surrender to the Japanese and went to Harbin to meet with Honjo, participating in Honjo's plan to establish a puppet state and obtaining its secrets. Then he severed relations with Honjo and announced its secrets to the world. The Japanese military閥 was very resentful of Komai's miscalculation and attacked him fiercely. Komai submitted his resignation in mid-June because of this. In fact, it was out of temporary anger. From then on, the opinions of the Japanese military閥 and the civilian faction deviated further and further. The military閥 and Manchurian ruffians believed that Manchuria was a Japanese territory, and everything had to be obeyed by the Japanese, especially under the command of the Japanese military閥. The civilian officials represented by Komai wore masks and vigorously advocated that Manchuria was an independent country and should not be interfered with, nor should Japanese people monopolize its agencies, arousing international disgust. They also said that if the Japanese regarded Manchuria as a territory, it was difficult to guarantee that there would be no second anti-Japanese leader like Ma Zhanshan, so they tried to stop it in every way. The Japanese military閥 hated this very much. However, at that time, the puppet dignitaries secretly hated the arrogance of the Japanese military people, and they all stood up to support Komai in order to maintain their temporary face. Although the Japanese military department was very dissatisfied with Komai, it did not take drastic action because the environment was not yet mature and feared that internal cracks would cause adverse consequences. Therefore, on the surface, they still persuaded Komai to do his best. However, from then on, the Japanese military department's surveillance of the puppet state officials became stricter. The appointment of an official in the puppet foreign ministry can be used as an example to illustrate this. Recently, someone who works as a clerk in the puppet foreign ministry must find four guarantors to ensure that he will not oppose Japan while in office and will not leave the East Province for mainland China after retirement. If there is any violation, the guarantors will be jointly liable before he can be hired. Others, such as section chiefs, police chiefs, or regimental commanders or brigade commanders, all have so-called Japanese advisers who supervise them. Nothing can be implemented without the signature of the Japanese adviser. Therefore, the puppet state has deep grievances against the Japanese military閥, but they have no choice in this situation. If a Japanese-Russian incident occurs, or the National Government sends troops to recover lost territory, they will surely turn against them and respond to the National Army. Therefore, the conflict between the civilian officials and the military閥 is getting deeper and deeper, and Komai's handling is becoming more and more difficult. This is another reason why Komai had to submit his resignation.

4. Financial Resources Have Reached the End of the Road

Benevolent Words but Ruthless Exactions

Since the September 18th Incident in the three northeastern provinces last year, the war and chaos have not stopped for a single day. The land is full of smoke and fire, cities and towns are in ruins, people have died tragically, and crops have failed. The entire land is like a hell. In order to co-opt the people, the Japanese ordered puppet officials to promote their meager taxes and the politics of the royal way everywhere, in order to cover up the situation of thousands of holes and hundreds of sores caused by their military force. However, the people are still mostly resistant to paying taxes. Therefore, the finances of the puppet state have reached the end of the road. The military expenditure is increasing day by day, and the anti-Japanese sentiment of the people is also increasing. In addition, the industries in various places have been occupied by the Japanese, and the positions in the government offices have also been seized by the Japanese. From top to bottom, the anti-Japanese situation is brewing more and more intensely. If the current situation cannot be dealt with, the puppet organization in the Northeast will not be far from its end. In order to cope with the difficult financial situation, the puppet organization is desperately demanding that the Japanese government recognize the puppet organization, and then sign a treaty, sell the country, and ask Japan for loans to save the current crisis. In fact, the Japanese have many differences in the views of the military閥 and the civilian faction on this financial crisis. This is also one of the reasons why Komai had to submit his resignation. From this observation, it can be seen that the puppet state is surrounded by crises. Taking the financial issue as an example, the Japanese government is unable to take care of itself, so how can it have the ability to cope with the crisis of the puppet state? Moreover, there is an internal opposition between the civilian and military factions, and an external bloody battle with the Volunteer Army. From now on, the affairs of the Northeast are really unbearable to ask. (21, 7, 27)

Reward Offered for the Capture of He Long

Chiang Rewards Xu Yuanquan's Troops with 45,000 Yuan

And Cables to Bandit Suppression Troops in Three Provinces to Relentlessly Suppress

Hankou Correspondence: Since the recovery of Qianjiang and the relief of Zao City, He Long's remnants have no foothold on the north and south banks of the Xiang River. They have reorganized the pseudo 7th, 8th, 9th, and 3rd Divisions, using regiments as units, and fled in all directions. He Long himself led the 7th and 8th Divisions, passing through Tai Li Temple and Lower Yang Port, and retreated to the Maliangji area west of the Xiang River. Xu Yuanquan, the Deputy Commander of the Left Route Army, is personally supervising the 48th Division, the 44th Division of Xiao Zhichu, the 41st Division of Zhang Zhenhan, the 13th Division of Wan Yaohuang, and the 37th Brigade of Liu Peixu, as well as coordinating with the Sichuan Army to pursue and suppress the bandits in different directions. According to reports, the bandits have indeed broken into small groups, and internal divisions are also emerging. Those who bring weapons to surrender are constantly appearing along the road. After receiving the telegram, He replied to the Chairman of the Provincial Government, Xia Douyin, on the 27th, stating that he was willing to make efforts to raise funds and must obtain the chief culprit, and at the same time ordered the Financial Department to raise funds for use. The provincial and municipal party departments and the Wuhan chambers of commerce also held a joint meeting on the 29th to discuss ways to comfort the bandit suppression soldiers who were fighting in the hot summer, and decided to organize a comfort society, assuming 20,000 yuan as comfort money to raise from all parties. Under the heavy rewards, commendations, and comforts, the morale of the bandit suppression soldiers has been boosted, and it should not be a problem to eliminate the remnants of the bandits. As for the expenses for suppressing bandits, the provincial government bears a heavy burden. Although the provincial treasury is in dire straits, it cannot but make efforts to raise funds to meet this urgent need. In addition to implementing an increase in the regular amount of land tax to supplement the provincial treasury's deficit, a committee for expediting payments has been organized jointly with the Pacification Commissioner's Office to expedite the payment of public bonds raised by the gentry and wealthy people in charge of the Clean Village Promotion Association. On the 29th, the association sent a letter to the Clean Village Promotion Association, requesting that the names, addresses, and amounts raised from each household that has not paid be sent for collection. Plan After Zhu and Mao's Failed Attempt to Invade Guangdong

Kong's Bandits Also Attempt to Break Out of Hubei Eastward from Northern Jiangxi

Because Nankang,

Eastern Section of the Longhai Railway 90

Road Construction and Port Development Underway

Road Construction Project Largely Complete

Port Development Plan Awaits the Coming Year

Xuzhou Correspondence: The problem of developing a port at Hugou in the eastern section of the Longhai Railway has been discussed for a long time, so the railway bureau is actively proceeding with the extension of the Xin-Xu railway line. Some time ago, it sent the Chief of the General Affairs Section, Yu Shibin, to the sea to inspect everything. According to his conversation when passing through Xuzhou upon his return to Zhengzhou, the road construction project in the eastern section is divided into three sections. The first section runs southeast from Xinpu to Hugou, about 24 kilometers long. This section is entirely earthwork, contracted out to bidders and calculated by the square measure. The second section, from Hugou to Lao Yao, is about 15 kilometers long and entirely stonework. Passing through Sunjia Mountain, it is necessary to excavate a cave and build a tunnel, also contracted out. Near Lao Yao, a seaport dock is being built, as the third section. In total, from Xinpu Dapu to the terminal point, the length is about 56 Chinese miles. The earthwork in the first section is very easy, and it can be completed in three or four months. The second section is more laborious and will take six or seven months to complete. The third section is purely port development work, building the Lao Yao dock, which must be a peninsula-style dock, capable of accommodating 3,000-ton ships on all three sides. It is also necessary to build railway tracks on both sides of the dock, so that passengers and goods can be directly moved without the effort of transfer. The port development plan first involves dredging the silt in the port to ensure that heavy-laden ships can pass smoothly. In the future, the eastern Lian Island in the east will be connected to the old dock by a seawall, forming a unified whole and serving as a dry dock. Then its prosperity will be comparable to Hong Kong and Qingdao. At present, the road construction project is progressing very quickly. The railway has purchased two small steamers specifically for transporting materials, transporting them from Dapu along the coast to Lao Yao, some for building stone bridges and tunnels, and some for preparing materials for port development. This time, the extension of the railway line faces economic difficulties, so a section of the abandoned Qingyang Railway branch line has been dismantled, borrowing a large number of railway track materials to pave the Xin-Xu railway line. However, it is still necessary to purchase more than 100,000 yuan worth of sleepers. The railway work is estimated to be around 400,000 yuan. If all kinds of materials are calculated at the total cash required, excluding port development, the various projects will also require around 2 million yuan. Currently, the road construction project is not a problem, and the port development plan will continue next year. (July 29th)

Jiang Dingwen

Prohibition of Opium, Prostitution, and Gambling in Bengbu 91

Prostitutes Ordered to Leave the Territory by a Deadline

Opium and Gambling Absolutely Prohibited

Bengbu Correspondence: In recent years, Bengbu's morals have been declining, and the root cause lies in the three evils of opium, prostitution, and gambling. Public prostitutes are renamed singing girls, and the Public Security Bureau collects "clear singing donations" from them to subsidize police salaries, which can amount to four or five thousand yuan per month. However, the singing girls still mainly engage in prostitution, with singing being only incidental. There are no fewer than six or seven hundred public and private prostitutes in the entire city, so brothels are everywhere. Moreover, opium dens are densely packed, and gambling halls are open, especially serving as places to hide petty criminals. Previously, opium dens were taxed by the government through lamp taxes, and gambling halls were taxed by bureau heads. Since Xu Tingyao was ordered to eliminate opium donations, opium taxes have no longer been collected, but open-air gambling is still unavoidable. Therefore, disputes and fights due to gambling among demobilized soldiers, ruffians, and vagrants in the entertainment venues occur almost daily. Jiang Dingwen, the commander of the Bengbu Garrison, recently convened a garrison meeting and had a detailed discussion on the prohibition of opium, prostitution, and gambling. Jiang advocated the complete prohibition of prostitutes, gambling, opium, and drug pills to restore declining morals. Today (28th), he specifically issued an order to implement it, ordering all public and private prostitutes in Bengbu to leave the territory by the end of July, and absolutely prohibiting gambling, opium, red and white pills, etc., from today. He also ordered military and police agencies and troops to strictly enforce the order, without favoritism or concealment, in order to completely prohibit these activities. (28th)

Local Correspondence

Songjiang 92

Songjiang Bank Creditors to Receive 10% Payout

After the collapse of Songjiang Bank in February amidst the war in Shanghai, depositors and savers formed creditor groups and filed lawsuits, alleging that the bank president, Xie Liangda, had fled with his family, and that the directors and supervisors should be responsible for repayment. The court designated an accountant to handle the liquidation and sent letters to all debtors to demand repayment. Not only were few repayments received, but many unsecured debts were found, clearly indicating fraud by the bank's executives. The liquidation office is now selling off houses and government bonds, with the proceeds sufficient to distribute a 10% payout. The payment is scheduled to begin on August 5th. Previously, after the Education Bureau's Asset Management Office requested the seizure of President Xie's residence and land, Xie's relative, Mr. Xie Yu, filed a lawsuit in court, raising an objection to the enforcement. The reason given was that the houses and land were jointly owned by the brothers and had not yet been divided, so the brothers should not be affected by Xie Liangda's actions. The lawsuit filed by Zhang Zuo, Liu Zhu Jing, and Lü, representatives of the creditor group, was heard in court yesterday. The directors and supervisors appointed lawyer Sha Xunyi to appear in court as their representative, while the creditor group appointed lawyers Liu Zhimou and Zhai Yue to appear in court. After the interrogator investigated the facts in detail, he ordered the liquidation office to provide a further report for review. It is said that the savings depositors' creditor group will also entrust lawyers to file a lawsuit.

This County Implements the Righteous Community System on a Trial Basis 93

This county previously received an order from the province stating that national taxes were often retained and delayed by clerks and officials, and that to rectify this, the righteous community system of Wuxi and other counties should be adopted and implemented immediately. The county submitted this to the fifth administrative meeting, which resolved to order each district to designate areas to promote a trial implementation, requiring one-third to be completed first. The first district office has designated Huayang Town, Baiwo Temple Township, Dongxinbang Township, Xinhe Road Township, Jingxin Township, Zhuangjiabang Township, Chenjiabang Township, Sixiangang Township, Xuejiayan Township, Dongwai Town, and Beiwai Town as areas for the righteous community trial implementation, and has reported this to the county government for record. According to the righteous community system, ten wealthy households within the community are selected to take turns each year to be responsible for the collection of national taxes in the community. The selected households may not refuse and must enter into a righteous community contract to ensure compliance. It is said that the implementation in Wuxi has been quite effective.

Zhangze Chamber of Commerce Provides Free Preventive Injections 94

Zhangze Town Chamber of Commerce Chairman Wang Songzhi, in view of the epidemic, started providing free preventive emergency injections on August 1st, entrusting renowned doctors to administer the injections, and displaying various epidemic prevention posters throughout the town to raise public awareness.

Kunshan 95

Detectives Stationed in Shanghai Arrest Kidnappers

The families of Wang Hanchen and Zhou Zhicheng in Pingzhuangtian, Bacheng, were robbed by a large gang of bandits last month. Before leaving, the bandits kidnapped Zhou Zhicheng and others. Afterwards, letters were received from the bandits demanding a large sum of money. The victims ignored the bandits' excessive demands. Two months later, the gang of bandits hid near a certain university in Jiangwan. After being discovered by Quan Lin, a detective stationed in Shanghai from this county, the Municipal Public Security Bureau was notified, and Patrol Officer Kong Fanren of the Zhabei Water Police Second Team led police to arrest them. Three bandit boats and eight bandits, including Wu Xiaoxizi, Zhou Xiaomazi, and You Xiaodeng, were arrested in the river. Fifty rounds of rifle ammunition were confiscated. Upon learning this, Director Tai of the County Public Security Bureau prepared a document on the 29th and sent Officer Chen and police to escort them back. They were brought back to Kunshan at 5 PM. Section Chief Xia interrogated them one by one. Because there were fifty or sixty accomplices in the case and the hostages had not yet been rescued, the matter was kept secret temporarily. The bandits were detained, and the county government was informed for questioning. Efforts are underway to apprehend the escaped bandits for punishment.

Rampant Epidemic, Successive Deaths

The epidemic in the urban and rural areas of this county is even more rampant, with more than ten deaths occurring daily. In the family of Zhang in the northern township, five family members suffered three deaths in a row. The wife of Ling Wenzhi and her eldest daughter in the west gate died from the epidemic on the same day. Yan Liu in the east gate died in less than an hour. It is truly tragic.

Suzhou 97

False Alarm on the Su-Chang Steamer

The Lao Gongmao Su-Chang steamer, which returned from Changshu the other day, carried patrol boat No. 6 of the 13th team of the 3rd district of the water police. When it reached a place near Likou, a white-hulled steamship suddenly approached, carrying more than seventy soldiers with complete firearms. As soon as it reached the side of the steamer, they jumped aboard the company's ship and circled to patrol boat No. 6, successively moving objects to the steamship. Among them was a box of bullets, with the words "bullet box" written on the surface, but it was unknown what was actually in the box. Before leaving, they also took the patrol officer of patrol boat No. 6 aboard the steamship and left. The authorities are now vigorously investigating the case, hoping to find out the truth.

Conclusion of Arguments in the Xu-Ma Lawsuit 98

Ma Baolin, the young owner of Ma Yuanji Satin Shop, and his fiancée, Xu Caizhen, committed suicide by poisoning. Xu Caizhen insisted on guarding her chastity at the Ma family after her husband's death. On the 11th of this month, it was Dou Lin's death anniversary, and Caizhen and her mother went to the Ma family to pay their respects, but were refused by Ma Zhang, Ma's aunt, causing a scuffle. Afterwards, Ma Zhang sued Caizhen for trespassing and assault. The Wuxian County Court opened a hearing on the 25th to mediate a reconciliation between the two parties. Subsequently, Xu Tang and her daughter Xu Caizhen sued Ma Zhang for assault and opium. After the prosecutor filed a public prosecution, the court, presided over by Judge Yang, held a hearing yesterday (30th). The plaintiff, Xu Tang, voluntarily withdrew the assault charge. Regarding the opium charge, Judge Yang repeatedly questioned Ma Zhang, who only admitted to occasionally smoking it in the past. Subsequently, the prosecutor made his argument, and the defendant's lawyers, Lu Hongyi, Gu Enpei, and Zhou Yuqin, made their defense. As a result, the court announced the conclusion of the arguments in the case and scheduled the verdict for August 1st.

Wuxi 99

Request to Borrow and Levy Grain Storage Funds

County Magistrate Chen of this county stated that the grain storage funds in this county had not been collected since 1920. The county government had repeatedly requested permission, but it was restricted by the 1% surtax, and permission could not be obtained. As of the end of June this year, only 20,000 yuan remained in these funds. Now, due to the urgent need for disaster relief, permission has been granted by the provincial government to borrow these funds. However, the entire population of Wuxi is more than 940,000, and many of them are poor farmers who urgently need relief. How can this amount be sufficient? Moreover, for future disaster preparedness, it is necessary to plan ahead. Therefore, it is proposed to temporarily borrow and levy the land price tax of one jiao per mu for the second term of this year, which was originally intended to be used for surveying expenses, for grain storage funds, limited to one time only, specifically for disaster preparedness. This measure is purely for the purpose of shifting funds to meet urgent needs, and what is taken from the people will still be used for the people. The local people should be able to understand this. The matter has been submitted to the 147th county administrative meeting and resolved, and the county has requested the provincial government for approval.

Jiangyin 100

Security Regiment Stationed in Cheng奉令调通

The coastal area of Lvsi, Nantong, is rampant with pirates. Although it has gradually become peaceful after the provincial security department sent a guerrilla team to defend it, there are still small groups of pirates who often appear in remote ports along the river and sea, such as Gao, Hai, Men, Chongming, Qidong, and Liuhaisha. They demand ransoms and smuggle guns, which are quite active. The Provincial Security Department has decided to调江阴安保第一团開通。 After receiving the order, the regiment commander, Zhu Mian, will, within about a week, send the first and second battalions and the mortar company stationed in Cheng to Tong via the Yangtze River. The third battalion of Pingwang and the fourth battalion of Changshu will go to Tong from Fukou, stationed in Sanjia Town, Tongru, and other places. In Jiangyin, a part will be left for defense.

Farmer Blown Up Due to Unrecognized Shell 101

Xu San, a farmer from Qiuxin Township, Shazhou, Third District, found a mortar shell while cutting grass in the fields in March. It was shaped like a hammer. Xu San did not recognize it and placed it on top of the pigsty. It had been there for several months. Strong winds had been blowing for days, and the pigsty collapsed. At 2 PM on the 28th, Xu San was rebuilding the pigsty when he saw the shell still there. He wanted to know what it was, so he struck it hard with a wooden stick. With a loud bang, shrapnel flew in all directions, piercing his abdomen. His back and arms were blown off. His family rushed him to the hospital for treatment, but he died on the way.

Zhenjiang 102

Jiangsu Province Promotes Cooperative Chicken Farming

The Jiangsu Department of Industry and Commerce believes that the chicken farming business is suitable for both specialized operation and farmers' sideline business. County governments should encourage farmers to consider local conditions, adopt cooperative methods, organize chicken farming cooperatives, jointly purchase chicks, jointly raise them, and jointly transport and sell chicken eggs and chickens, in order to promote agricultural production. It has specially compiled a model charter for such cooperatives and ordered the county governments to follow it.

Provincial Government Restricts Surtaxes on Land Tax 103

The provincial government believes that in recent years, the surtaxes on land tax in various places have been several times higher than the regular tax, and the burden on the people has increased year after year. If strict restrictions are not imposed, it will not be enough to show caution and consideration. It is now stipulated that from the 21st year onwards, if any county increases the burden on the people, it must first submit the undertaking to the competent department for approval. If there are no violations, it will be submitted to the provincial government for discussion, in order to show restrictions and reduce the burden on the people. The above order has been issued to the departments for transmission to the counties for compliance.

Yangzhou 104

Continued Collapse of the Jiang'an Riverbank in Liuwei

The Jiang'an Riverbank in Liuwei, Jiaxing Bridge, a part of the city, has collapsed repeatedly in recent years. Now, from 5 PM on the 27th to 8 PM on the 28th, it collapsed more than 60 zhang to the north and more than 20 zhang to the west, starting from the river mouth. Fortunately, when it cracked, the staff of the Zhenjiang-Yangzhou Motor Vehicle Liuwei Station, as well as passengers and farmers, all saw it and rushed to dismantle houses and move things, saving about 70%. The remaining losses to fields and land are estimated at 60,000 to 70,000 gold. The materials for the motor vehicle station that fell into the river also amounted to more than 300 yuan. This morning (29th), cracks appeared in the uncollapsed areas, making further collapses inevitable. Fortunately, no one has been injured yet. Currently, the river mouth is only three li away from the Hongqiao Bridge. Passengers taking buses to the ferry all use the company's barges to be transported to the original ferry landing at the river mouth and walk more than 20 zhang before boarding the ferry. This is because the old bank of the river mouth still has a dike, and the ferry cannot reach the new river mouth.

Two Police Squadrons to Be Abolished

County Magistrate Yang Zirong previously submitted a request to the Department of Civil Affairs to abolish the first and second squadrons of the police force, but it has not yet been approved. It is now heard that a decision has been made to abolish them starting on August 1st. All of the police force will be reorganized into six squads, directly under the command of the brigade headquarters.

Public Security Branch Not Temporarily Abolished

The ten branches of the Jiangdu Public Security Bureau, due to financial difficulties, were unanimously resolved by the participating groups to be abolished during the review of the budget for the 21st year and transformed into substations. County Magistrate Yang believed that this measure could effectively remedy the current shortage of public security funds. However, Director Chen of the Public Security Bureau requested instructions from the department because the substations could not directly detain or fine people. It is now heard that the Department of Civil Affairs also believes that changing the police system is not something that Jiangdu County can do on its own, and that the Ministry of Interior is currently comprehensively planning to improve the unified methods of public security in various provinces. All matters related to reorganization should be awaited until the ministry issues orders for compliance. Therefore, the previous plan to abolish and merge the Jiangdu branches is temporarily difficult to implement.

Gaoyou 105

Project Acceptance of the Canal Dike

The canal dike in northern Jiangsu has been completed. The Jiangsu Provincial Government specially united with the relevant agencies to organize the acceptance committee of the canal dike project in northern Jiangsu. The acceptance committee members departed from Yangzhou on the 16th of this month to accept the project works in the Huai-Pi section, Gao-Bao section, and Jiangdu section. The works of the upper reaches of the canal have been accepted. The committee members arrived in Gaoyou at 8 PM on the 26th and have been busy accepting the Gaoyou Pan East-West Dike. The reporter visited the West Dike office last night (27th) and met with the acceptance committee members, asking about the progress of the acceptance work. Acceptance committee member Dong Bochun detailed the progress as follows: The committee members departed from Yangzhou on the 16th of this month, arrived in Qingjiangpu on the evening of the 17th, and began accepting the works in the Shuangjin Gate area on the 18th. On the 19th, they accepted the embankment and the project works in the Sanke River and Hongze Lake Dam area. On the 20th, the committee members were divided into two groups to accept the embankment works from Qingjiang to Huaicheng. The first group, consisting of committee members Dong Bochun, Chen Bomeng, and Xu Decheng, accepted the East Dike. The second group, consisting of committee members He Haiqiao, Shen Baojun, and Shen Binyan, accepted the West Dike. On the 21st, they accepted the East-West Dike from Huaicheng to Pingqiao. On the 22nd, they accepted the East-West Dike from Pingqiao to Zhaoying. On the 23rd, they accepted the East-West Dike from Baoying to Sishui. On the 24th, they accepted the East-West Dike from Sishui to Jieshou. On the 25th, they accepted the East-West Dike from Jieshou to Mapengwan. The committee members arrived in Gaoyou at 8 PM on the 26th, staying at the West Dike office and Ma Junqing's residence. On the 27th, they accepted the East-West Dike from Mapengwan to Dangjunlou. From 7 AM to 1 PM on the 28th, they accepted the West Dike from Shaolongwan to Yuehegang. At 4 PM, they accepted the East Dike from Fengshen Temple to Pipa Gate. They plan to accept the Dangjunlou, Hehuatang, Qigongdian, and Yumatou breaches on the 29th. The acceptance is expected to be completed by August 5th. However, the engineering in the Huai-Pi section, with the 清江汎 being the simplest, 平桥堤工 being the best. In the Gao-Bao section of the Baoying, the 临城 is the worst. The engineering in Baoying is not up to standard. Regarding the dike工程 with insufficient dimensions, according to the opinions of the committee members, it is proposed to deduct their earthwork price. Also, although the dimensions of the Gaoyou汎 West Dike are not far from the prescribed ones, there are many cracks. The committee members believe that this section of the engineering is too insubstantial and plan to discuss a remedy. Regarding the four breaches north of Gaoyou city, although we have not yet accepted them, we took the opportunity to look at them yesterday. The engineering at Yumatou and Qigongdian is the best, while the engineering at Hehuatang is not very good. The engineering at Dangjunlou is the worst, and a crack suddenly appeared in that place the day before yesterday. Four of the committee members insisted on not accepting the sweeping engineering at that breach.

Rugao 106

Exemption of Additional Taxes on Newly Reclaimed Wasteland

The county government of this county recently received an order from the Department of Finance stating that the handling of supplementary grain assessment in this county has been underway for a long time, but the number of reports has not been high. The reason is that the additional taxes levied under the land tax have gradually increased. If this is not slightly changed, it will not be conducive to progress. It is now decided that from now on, regardless of whether it is newly reclaimed wasteland or privately owned beachland, the newly reported tax assessments will be exempt from all additional taxes for three years from the date of the report, in order to show consideration. The county government has issued a notice to this effect for public knowledge.

Xiaoshan 107

Farmers Engage in Armed Clashes Over Fishing

In Wangcun, the fourth district of Xiaoshan, farmers Wang Caifa and Zhang Jicheng, who live nearby, had a verbal dispute over draining water from a pond to catch fish, which then turned violent. On the night of the 27th, the Wang family gathered many people, each holding knives and spears, and attacked the Zhang family's village. The Zhang family also gathered twenty or thirty people, each holding sharp weapons, and confronted them. As a result, two people from the Wang family were injured by knives, and one person from the Zhang family was injured. It is heard that the injured from the Wang family are all in critical condition and their lives may be in danger. Both sides have been taken to the county court for examination, and it is unknown how the matter will be resolved.

Tobacco Leaves and Green Ramie Enjoy a Bumper Harvest This Year

The area in the western township of Xiaoshan, where tobacco leaves are produced, sells no less than tens of thousands of gold worth of tobacco leaves to tobacco companies in Shanghai and Hangzhou every year. This year, the weather during the summer dog days has been clear and sunny, and the tobacco leaves have dried to a bright yellow color when sun-dried. The green ramie grown in the sandy soil has also had a very abundant harvest, and the price is also very high. Usually, a large quantity is sold overseas. This large income for the farmers there is a small contribution to the rural economy.

Hangzhou 108

Sentencing of Tao Sijin's Appeal

In the case of the appeal of Tao Sijin, a female student at the art school, who tragically killed her classmate Liu Mengying, the Criminal Division One of the Zhejiang High Court summoned witnesses for interrogation on the 26th and concluded the case. This morning (30th), the defendant Xu Qinwen and the plaintiff Liu Qingxing were both absent when the court officer was ordered to bring Tao Sijin from the detention center. Court President Jin Wen'e then read the main text of the judgment: In the case of Tao Sijin's premeditated murder appeal and Liu Qingxing's incidental civil appeal, the original judgment, except for the part concerning the incidental civil part which was revoked, Tao Sijin was sentenced to death for premeditated murder; Xu Qinwen was sentenced to two years of fixed-term imprisonment for intending to commit adultery and enticing a woman under the age of twenty to leave the person who enjoys parental rights. Liu Qingxing's incidental civil lawsuit was dismissed. It is heard that Tao's family and Xu Qinwen are both dissatisfied with the judgment and plan to appeal to the Supreme Court again.

Important News on Educational Administration of the Municipal Council 110

The issue of subsidies for private schools: According to news from the Information Office of the Municipal Council, the Committee on Subsidies for Chinese Private Schools has drafted several suggestions, which have been approved in principle by the Education Committee. However, before submitting the subsidy list to the Board of Directors, the Education Bureau's suggestions and the Chinese Education Director's report on the economic conditions of the schools and the subsidy fee method should be translated into English for reference. Furthermore, the Health Department should be requested to report on the sanitary conditions of each school. The Committee on Subsidies for Western Private Schools has drafted this year's subsidy list, which is generally in accordance with last year's methods. However, the 500 taels originally allocated to the Tilpen Family School for one year will be transferred to the William Emperor School. The Education Committee has approved this proposal, but will re-evaluate the amount given based on the situation of each school.

Proposed tuition increase for Chinese primary schools: At the Education Committee meeting on July 20th, the Director of Chinese Education suggested that, due to the high cost of building primary schools in the Western District and the relatively good economic conditions of the students' families, tuition fees should be increased from six yuan to twelve yuan per year, starting from the spring of next year. The situation is similar in the Northern District primary schools, and the same approach is planned. At the same time, it is proposed to increase the number of free students in both schools from one-tenth to two-tenths. For the Eastern District primary schools, due to the large number of poor students, no increase is proposed. After deliberation, the committee decided that the Western and Northern District primary schools should increase tuition fees starting from February 1933. The amount of the increase and the number of additional free students will be considered later.

Selection of the principal for the Hanbury School: The Education Committee has received the names of 14 candidates for this position and decided that the Chairman of the Committee, Mrs. Leslie, one member of the Selection Committee, and the Acting Superintendent of Education will review them. During this period, the school affairs will still be handled by Mr. S. Hore as acting principal, and Mr. H. G. Huckstep will be asked to continue serving as the director of the dormitory. All of the above have been approved by the Board of Directors on the 29th.

Discussion on the school fee increase proposal: Regarding the proposal to increase tuition fees for various schools, a certain member previously drafted a plan to gradually increase fees for middle school and senior students, while not increasing fees for elementary school students. This method would only increase fees by about 7 percent. The Education Committee agreed to the principle of increasing fees several months ago. Therefore, four Chinese schools that did not receive subsidies in 1931 should not increase tuition fees for Chinese students this year. It was also stated that the increase in fees should be at the beginning of the year, but the justification for this was not sufficient. The Board of Directors has now approved the issuance of subsidies and set a goal of increasing tuition fees to one-third of the expenses. In addition, the recent hiring of high-salaried teachers and the drop in silver prices by the Bureau are all reasons why it has become necessary to increase tuition fees. After discussion, the Board of Directors decided on a compromise solution: starting from September this year, the tuition fees for each Chinese public school will be increased by four yuan, and another four yuan next year. The fee increase for each Western school will follow the original plan starting from the next semester. In addition, except for the exceptions listed by the committee, for students whose parents are not taxpayers in the concession, their tuition fees should be increased by one-quarter.

China Arts and Crafts Society 111

Inauguration Anniversary Art Exhibition

From August 1st to 7th, the inauguration anniversary art exhibition of the China Arts and Crafts Society's new location on Jin Shenfu Road will open to the public from 9:00 AM on August 1st. It will be divided into sections for Chinese painting, calligraphy, bronze and stone inscriptions, seal carving, Western painting, sculpture, and photography. The Chinese painting section will be further divided into rooms for ancient and modern paintings. The ancient painting room will display authentic works by famous painters from the Song, Yuan, Ming, and Qing dynasties. The modern painting room will feature exquisite works by over 40 contemporary masters such as Huang Binhong, Wang Yiting, Zhang Shanzi, Ma Mengrong, Chen Xiaodie, He Tianjian, Qian Shoutie, Zheng Wuchang, Zhang Daqian, Lou Xinhu, and Xie Gongzhan. The calligraphy, bronze and stone inscription, and seal carving section will feature artifacts from the Three Dynasties, statues from the Northern Wei Dynasty at Yungang, statues from the Northern Zhou Dynasty, gold and jade artifacts from various dynasties, ancient seals from the Six Dynasties, Tang Dynasty sutras, ancient jades from the Three Dynasties, ancient porcelains from the Song, Yuan, Ming, and Qing dynasties, and calligraphy and paintings from the Song, Yuan, Ming, and Qing dynasties. The treasures are treasured by Huang Binhong and others. The Western painting section will feature over a hundred masterpieces by Liu Haisu, Wang Jiyuan, Ni Yide, Pan Yuliang, Guan Liang, Wang Yuanbo, Zhang Xian, Pang Xunqin, and Zhang Chenbo, which are innovative and pioneering, opening up a new era for Western painting in our country. The sculpture section will feature recent works by Zhang Chenbo, Jiang Xiaojian, Yan Deyun, Chen Zhongshu, Wang Zaiyu, and others, including wood and stone carvings and plaster sculptures. The photography section, specially set up by the Shen Bao, will display over a hundred types of on-the-spot photographs of the Northeast Incident and the Shanghai January 28 Incident. The Commercial Press will display 60 photographs of destruction. There will also be over a hundred photographs of the Shanghai Incident taken by the Shanghai Federation of Patriotic Organizations and Liu Jiazeng, which will surely evoke patriotic sentiments among the Chinese people. The exhibition will be open until August 7th.

America Won Doubles Yesterday

France Currently Leads Two to One Reuters, Paris, 30th - In the second day of the Davis Cup Challenge Round doubles match, American players Allison and Van Ryn defeated French players Cochet and Brugnon by scores of 6-3, 11-13, 7-5, 4-6, 6-4.

France Sweeps Both Singles Reuters, Paris, 29th - In the Davis Cup America-France Challenge Round, France won both singles matches today, and is very likely to retain the cup for the sixth consecutive year. It is only necessary to win one more group out of the next three. Under the gaze of enthusiastic spectators, French veteran Borotra regained his youthful vigor and defeated American's top singles player Vines by scores of 6-4, 6-2, 3-6, 6-4. Borotra Versus Vines 116

6-4, 6-2, 3-6, 6-4

First Set At 2:15 PM, Borotra and Vines entered the court simultaneously, receiving enthusiastic cheers from the audience. Photographers and filmmakers competed to take pictures. After a draw, it was decided that Vines would serve first. The two practiced briefly before the official start of the match. Vines' shots, both forehand and backhand, were extremely accurate, giving him an advantage. However, Borotra rallied and regained balance. He won the first game. Borotra won again in the second game with a burst of energy. Vines won the third game, serving and defeating Borotra. In the fourth game, Borotra was troubled by his opponent and failed. At this point, Borotra and Vines had each won two games. Vines served quickly, and Borotra missed many balls, but then he quickly recovered, controlled the ball, and won the fifth game. Borotra then won two more games, taking a 5-2 lead. Vines sensed danger and worked hard to win two games, but Borotra ultimately won the first set 6-4.

Second Set At the beginning, Borotra seemed to have returned to his prime. His ball skills were amazing. Although Vines tried to control his enemy, he was ineffective. Borotra's shots became more rapid. Those who admired him were very happy. Borotra won the first two games. He failed in the third game. Then he again won two for a score of four to two. The balls he hit were long, straight and true. Vines continued running back and forth, but still failed to return the serve. Borotra won the second set 6-2.

Third Set At this point, Vines knew he should try to make a great effort. But he lost the first game. Borotra seemed to have a slight sign of tiredness. Vines took the victory with a score of 6-3.

Fourth Set Both players rested for a while according to the practice. In the fourth set, Borotra followed his old technique and it seemed to have a positive result. But Vines won three straight games taking a 3-1 lead. Then, Borotra displayed his special skills. His shots were as fast as lightning and so precise. Both forehand and backhand shots landed on the edges of the court. Although Vines ran back and forth, he could not defend. Borotra won two straight games, and the score was tied. At this moment, the ball moved extremely fast. Observers were animated. The observers cheered and applauded every good shot. Vines' spirit waned, and his shots became sluggish. Borotra won the fourth set 6-4. In total, through four sets, Borotra was victorious with scores of 6-4, 6-2, 3-6, 6-4.

The 10th World Games Opened Yesterday 123

Liu Changchun Participated to Promote National Glory

The Opening Ceremony Was Held at 2 PM, the US Vice President Gave the Opening Speech

36 Countries of Male and Female Heroes Participated in the International Parade Ceremony

The 10th World Olympic Games was held at 2 PM yesterday at the Olympic Competition Arena in Los Angeles, California, USA. US Vice President Curtis gave the opening speech and officially declared the opening. After the ceremony, weightlifting competitions began at 6 PM.

(1) The Grandeur of the Opening Ceremony 124

38 Countries Participated

Los Angeles, 30th - The 10th World Olympic Games opened today. The venue was filled with 105,000 spectators. National flags of the participating countries were hoisted around the venue. At 2:25 PM, Honorary President of the Games, Vice President Curtis, entered the venue. At this time, a military band of 2,000 people played the US anthem. Then, the athletes' entry ceremony was held. The Greek athletes were the first to enter, and the American athletes were the last. Athletes from 38 countries marched into the arena, holding their national flags high. They lined up in front of the Honorary President's seat. First, Organizing Committee Chairman Garrot took the oath, followed by Honorary President Curtis, who declared the opening of the Games. Amidst the music played by the military band, a salute was fired, and the Games flag was slowly raised at the same time. Then, University of California President Dr. Spura gave a congratulatory speech. At 3:55 PM, the athletes from various countries went to the President's seat to raise their flags and take the oath. The ceremony then concluded. The athletes exited the arena, and the competitions began immediately. (Japan United) The 10th International Olympic Games, which brings together famous athletes from various countries, was opened by US Vice President Curtis at 2 PM today. Sports enthusiasts around the world thought that a stage for an international sports meeting that was hard to come by in a thousand years has just opened. The day was clear and the wind was calm. The crowds of visitors aimed at the sports field. Since morning, the asphalt streets have been crowded with cars. The trams and buses were all full of visitors. By noon, the sports field had already accommodated 100,000 spectators, and there was no room for another foot. Several tens of thousands of people were still outside the venue. At 3 PM, representative athletes from various countries gathered in the rest area, each preparing their teams, waiting for their arrival. At 2:30 PM, the US Vice President Curtis, representing the President, sang the US national anthem (Star-Spangled Banner) together. He arrived and sat in the front VIP seat.

(2) Liu Changchun and Song Junfu March 125

At 2:50 PM, more than 2,000 participating athletes began to enter the arena. The first was Greece, the birthplace of the Olympics, and the last was the host country, the United States. The athletes from the various countries in between were arranged in ABC order, circling the arena. Chinese athlete Liu Changchun, holding the Blue Sky with a White Sun flag presented by Wang Zhengting, and Song Junfu, appeared in the team. The whole group was divided into four columns, all with a determination to win, circling the arena. The distance between the teams from each country was 20 to 30 meters, forming a long snake shape. Each team entered the arena through the Marathon Gate. The sound of applause was deafening, mixed with the voices of people, resembling a symphony. The Japanese athletes and the Chinese athletes, the Japan support group and the Chinese community, each cheered. When the athletes walked in front of the Vice President on the central viewing platform, they took off their hats and looked to the right, showing respect. They went half a circle to the viewing stand. Each team placed its flag in the front in a predetermined location. At 3:40 PM, members of the International Olympic Committee and the US Olympic Association descended to the arena to invite Vice President Curtis to give a speech (the speech will be detailed separately). Then the music sounded, and a chorus of ten people sang the Olympic anthem. At that time, the Olympic flag was raised. At this time, ten salute shots were fired. The torch on the Olympic Tower, which included the venue, was ablaze. Two thousand doves, with national flags around their necks, flew over the sports arena. The arena was filled with a solemn and peaceful atmosphere. The music played a march. All of the national teams formed a semi-circle with the platform as the center, each with their flags facing forward. The American athlete Kana mounted the platform. With his left hand, he held the national flag, and with his right hand, he raised the Olympic oath. (We athletes, at the occasion of joining the Olympic Games, will respect the rules of sports, will follow the spirit of the knight in the games for the honor of our homeland, to participate in various sports with the honor of sports, this oath ...) More than two thousand athletes raised their right hands and recited the oath together. Then they circled the venue again. At 4:20 PM, the solemn opening ceremony of the Olympic Games ended. At that time, dozens of airplanes flew over the arena, adding color to the opening ceremony.

Free Talk

Nine Three Old Man Ma Xiangbo's Quotations

The Most Expensive Soup in the World 133

— Han Ji

A guest came from Paris. I asked him…

(Paris is the most prosperous place under heaven. May I ask, in a restaurant, how much does the most expensive soup cost?)

The guest replied… (Perhaps, at most, it wouldn’t exceed fifty francs?) I said… (Fifty francs is far too cheap!) (Then, a hundred francs for a bowl, that soup is probably the most expensive in Paris?) the guest said with some embarrassment. I repeatedly shook my head, saying: (Still too cheap! In a prosperous place like Paris, a bowl of elaborate soup is only worth a hundred francs, that’s really too cheap!)

Hearing this, the guest was speechless, and asked for the reason. I smiled and said:

(One day, Zhiyao (Mr. Zhu Zhiyao is the wise nephew of Prime Minister Xiang) accompanied me out for a snack at a restaurant. As soon as I sat down and opened the menu, I suddenly saw a soup on the soup list called Sun Yat-sen Soup, priced at six hundred silver dollars. I was shocked when I saw it, stunned to the point of being unable to speak. After a long while, I repeatedly shook my head, feeling it was really too expensive. I was afraid this bowl of Sun Yat-sen Soup was the most expensive soup in the world!

(Later, there was no way around it, soup had to be drunk after all, so I ordered a cheaper soup from the soup list, which still cost five dollars. Tasting it, I also found it very boring, with not much flavor!)

Upon hearing this, the guest was shocked and said:

(In a prosperous place like Paris, I have never seen soup worth five hundred dollars. I see that Shanghai's prosperity is advancing a thousand miles a day, and it seems that Paris is not as good as Shanghai! ) I listened and just nodded, not committing one way or the other. The expensiveness of the soup? Or the prosperity of Shanghai? This is my riddle.

Japan's Old Method 134

— Tian Hen

Now that Japan has occupied the entire Manchuria, the military era is almost over, and we are entering an era of annexation. The so-called "Manchukuo" is just a clever trick to ease international tensions. In the minds of the Japanese, they can't wait to annex it as soon as possible. Therefore, in the past month, the movement to unify the four-headed government and the efforts to seize salt tax, customs duties, and postal rights have been proceeding simultaneously. Once the four-headed government is unified and the salt, customs, and post are all seized, the fate of the puppet Manchukuo will come to an end. It absolutely will not be prolonged for long, unless our government has the determination to recover it by force. Taking advantage of the fact that the volunteer army is now all over the Northeast, resolutely send troops to the Northeast, then Japan's dream of annexing Manchuria may not be realized. Now that the Japanese government is unifying the four-headed government, isn't it determined to establish a plenipotentiary government or a governor-general's office in Manchuria, and is the governor-general's office said to be very powerful? This is the old method of annexing Korea. They want to use the same method to deal with Manchuria. People will recall that the fall of Korea to the governor-general's office is as clear as if it were happening right now, because it hasn’t been that long. It was after the Russo-Japanese War that Korea completely became Japan's vassal state. Japan immediately took the opportunity to abolish the embassy stationed in Korea and re-established a governor-general's office, taking over all of Korea's diplomatic and internal affairs. However, the Japanese are extremely ruthless. Not satisfied, they took the opportunity to claim that the Korean king had secretly sent envoys to seek assistance from the Hague Peace Conference, and forced Korea to recognize the following conditions: (1) The governor-general has the power to guide the Korean government in its administration. (2) Laws and administration concerning Korea must be approved by the governor-general. (3) The promotion and demotion of high-ranking officials must be approved by the governor-general. (4) The governor-general may recommend Japanese people to be Korean officials, who shall be appointed by the Korean government. (5) Without the consent of the governor-general, no foreigners may be hired. Later, because of Ahn Jung-geun's assassination in Harbin, Japan added 20,000 police officers within Korea. Thus, on August 22nd of the second year of the Xuantong reign of the Qing Dynasty, the merger treaty was produced (Korea ceded all governing rights to Japan forever). This is a brief history of Japan establishing a governor-general's office before annexing Korea. Looking at it, which of the above five conditions is Japan and the puppet state lacking now? Even the police force is not lacking. There are 20,000 of them in Manchuria. The present Manchuria is exactly the same as Korea before the second year of Xuantong. It is only missing a governor-general's office (in fact, the governor-general's office already exists, only in a different name). Once the establishment is implemented, all the elements of annexation will be in place. It's just a matter of time. You traitors are still living in a drunken dream, willing to be puppets. Isn't that very sad?

Volunteer Youth 135

— Xie Lu

Since the Shanghai-Songhu Incident, the number of villagers fleeing back has been in the thousands every day. They are displaced and miserable, and their state is beyond description. One day, I was waiting for a guest at Cixi Railway Station. I saw a young man in military uniform and leather shoes, with a suave demeanor. Standing beside him was a beautiful young woman, covering her face and sobbing, murmuring something incomprehensible. The young man looked tall and proud, smoking a cigarette indifferently, and said to the woman with a smile, "Go quickly, go quickly. Don't bother me." The woman said, "Last winter, you went to Jinzhou to join the volunteer army. More than two hundred and seventy people went with you. Some died in the artillery fire, and some died from the severe cold. Now that you have returned alive, how can you bear to abandon your wife and children and re-enter the hail of bullets? Our family has several acres of farmland outside the city, which is enough to support ourselves. Even if you don't think about me, don't you think about your white-haired, doddering old mother? Yesterday, when she heard of your return, she was overjoyed and hugged you and cried. Now that you have been out for one night, you want to go to Shanghai and join the volunteer army. Your ambition is admirable, but what will I say to your old mother if she knows? I'm afraid she will die of grief. Even if you become an unknown hero, you will be an unfilial sinner." She cried loudly after speaking. The young man said, "When national disaster is upon us, I can't take care of filial love and personal feelings. My mind is made up. Why are you nagging? Moreover, everyone must die. Dying under the window is like Mount Tai compared to dying on the battlefield, which is like a feather. But life and death are also predetermined. I used to be a shop assistant at a store on Nanjing Road in Shanghai, earning no less than sixty or seventy dollars a month. Just because the powerful enemy is rampant and the Chinese people are living in a drunken dream, every time I read the newspaper, it makes me heartbroken. So I gathered more than two hundred and seventy comrades and rushed to the Northeast to join the volunteer army. At first, when I went to the battlefield, I was inevitably timid. After a long time, the fun suddenly arose. I even felt bored when I didn't fight fiercely with the enemy. Now, because of the severe cold in the Northeast, only one hundred and thirteen people have returned alive. Now the brutal bandits are even more ambitious, and they have invaded Shanghai-Songhu. I heard that the 19th Route Army can also fight back hard. If I don't go to the Northeast, I should also join Shanghai-Songhu, to deal with the brutal bandits. This is also the duty of every citizen. You should take good care of my mother and raise our son well. We'll have a good drink when we meet again in the future." At that time, the whistle sounded loudly. The Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo train had already snaked into the station. In the crowd, I only saw this volunteer youth jump into the train, waving his scarf to say goodbye to his wife.

Sitting in a Stuffy Movie Theater 136

— Zhou Shixun

In such hot weather, abandoning the clean and cool Yuyuan Road and sitting in a stuffy movie theater to watch a preview, I think this is the biggest sacrifice of my life. If the movie I'm watching isn't worth it, then this sacrifice won't be considered strange by others, but I may never forget it. Fortunately, this sacrifice is worth it.

The name of this film is "Love and Death." Produced by the Star Film Company, directed by Cheng Bugao. One of the main actors is Zhu Qiuhong, and the other is the very likeable little Zhang Zhiyun.

Imagery on the Yangtze River (Part 1) 137

— Shazhou

(1) The Flower Seller

I woke up at seven o'clock and saw from the window of a certain hotel in Xiaguan that four warships flying foreign flags were moored in the heart of the river. At the same time, the huge Wusong Jianglun steamer had also excitedly sailed in from the east. I was going to take this ship to Hankou, so I was washing my face in a hurry. Strangely, in the large mirror on the washstand, I saw a woman standing behind me. Her charming smile explained her intention. I hurriedly turned around and asked her, "What do you want?" She didn't answer, but picked two gardenia flowers from her handbag and gave them to me to smell. "Buy two fragrant ones, people going out need them," she said. As she spoke, her seductive, plump chest was gradually getting closer to me, so I had to say sternly, "Don't mess around, I'm about to board the ship. Don't you see who's here? Get out of here!" So she left unhappily, but she still had to walk into another room with a smile. When she walked out of the door, I seemed to see on her back: "Poor flower seller, I can't live by selling flowers."

(2) Passenger Life

The river steamer set sail, and I was already in the second-class cabin. The people seeing me off were looking at the ship sadly on the dock. The river wind was blowing into the cabin in gusts. The tea boy shouted loudly, "Machine gun is here!" Looking closely, I felt it was pitiful. It turned out that the so-called machine gun was just a bamboo pole more than a foot long. The muzzle only pointed at the gunner's mouth, and the bullets fired were real smoke bombs.

The opening of this machine gun aroused my interest in conducting a survey of the lives of passengers. So, after spending one hour and five minutes, I obtained the following statistics:

Playing mahjong: 28 people, reading newspapers: 15 people,

Reading magazines: 2 people, reading Infantry Drill Manual: 1 person,

Reading the History of Sexuality: 7 people (including 1 woman), washing clothes: 2 people,

Quarreling: 3 people, eating bread: 1 person,

Eating broad beans: 1 person, bragging: 6 people,

Operating machine guns: 74 people (distributed in 27 key locations),

Singing little songs while holding the railing: 1 person, writing statistical tables: 1 person

Note: The list above is limited to passengers, and the number of passengers looking at the river, chatting, sleeping, and going to the toilet is not included because they are countless.

The numbers on the right are based on my survey at the time. I am not responsible for any increases or decreases after the time.

I have not studied statistics, so the table is very sloppy.

Qian Ping. The male lead is Zheng Xiaoqiu. The main plot is to describe the sadness of a love triangle. The side plot is to highlight the errors of the marriage system. It's very ordinary, but after Bugao used his flexible and clever skills to direct it, it feels very tortuous and flavorful. Especially the aesthetic scenery, which has never been recorded in the Star Film Company, is even more eye-catching. Unexpectedly, in the midst of the storms and troubles of the Star Film Company, there would still be such a perfect product launched. This calm and composed attitude is also expressed in conjunction.

Finally, I hope that Star will put more effort into "new" things in the future. Otherwise, one product after another will be like a machine turning, without any vitality.

Striking the Bell at the Old Temple (60) 138

— Bu Chu Ting Cao Zhai Fu

Sixty-seven

(Go to the Northeast!)

(Take back the Northeast!)

These are new shouts that the old temple has never heard before... These shouts came from the hearts of the young people of the old temple, shaking the eardrums of all the people in the village, penetrating into the hearts of all the people in the village, causing all the people in the village to feel that (going to the Northeast) and (taking back the Northeast) had become a matter of course, believing that if they did not do so, they could not be considered Chinese people, nor could they be considered people of the old temple.

In the villages south of the Yangtze River, the popular motto is... (Good iron is not used to make nails... Good men do not become soldiers.) How could the people of the old temple not have been anesthetized by this kind of view of life? Why is it that now they not only approve of everyone becoming soldiers, but also want to deal with external violence on the battlefield? The thread of this psychological change is not difficult to find. Since the people of the old temple organized a self-defense group, they have already understood the greatness of the people's armed forces. Those bandits who cruelly tore up children not only dare not come again to rob, but they don't even dare to come and paste threatening letters, because of the effectiveness of life education, the people soon think of a country from a village. From the self-defense of the old temple, they jump to planning the self-defense of the whole country.

(Two people are too few, let's go together!) The young people with boiling blood said almost in unison at the meeting. Mr. Zhu spent a great deal of effort guiding us to use cold brains to command hot blood. He said... (Don't think it's too few that the old temple is sending these two strong men. In my opinion, these two people are no less than two million people. The mission of the old temple is to first fulfill its own responsibility, and then awaken one million villages across the country to fulfill the same responsibility. If each village sends two strong men, there will be two million elite soldiers, who can take on the mission of recovering the Northeast. If we send one more person, it can be considered that we are fulfilling one more responsibility, but at the same time, we are reducing the responsibility of other villages. Moreover, we must have a comprehensive plan to win. The farmland left behind by the village friends who have joined the army must be cultivated by us, and the entrusted old and young must be served and educated by us. Once we have spoken, it is difficult for even four horses to catch up. We must not issue blank checks to increase the worries of the soldiers defending the country, so I suggest that the quota for joining the army be temporarily set at two people, and if there is an urgent need in the future, it will be increased.) How are these two people to be allocated? There is no need to elect them. There are as many as thirteen people who volunteer. People

gave them a title, calling them the Thirteen Taibao of the Old Temple. The word "bao" (protect) has a broad meaning. What they protect is the entire Chinese nation, not the special interests of a few people. It is a little difficult to only send two of the Thirteen Taibao of the Old Temple. Some people advocate drawing lots. Some people advocate that the two young men with the fewest family burdens should go first. But the result is that none of the Thirteen Taibao are willing to stay at home. This is beyond Mr. Zhu's expectations! Mr. Zhu can call the young people to rise up, but he cannot call the young people who have already risen to sit down again. In the end, Mr. Zhu had to sacrifice his own proposal, and stepped up the training of the Thirteen Taibao day and night so that they could set off for the Northeast.

Yesterday (30th) at the Chinese Securities Exchange, the bond market situation was such that due to numerous rumors in the market, public sentiment was weak, leading to a surge in selling. Sudden Drop in Cotton Yarn Market, Prices Plunge 144

The cotton yarn market suddenly turned weak, with prices falling sharply. Large traders aggressively sold off their holdings, and the market has stalled after fulfilling a large amount of demand. As a result, bearish sentiment has become more active, and pressure has increased. Rumors circulated in the market that several thousand bales of No. 16 Tianjin cotton yarn were being shipped to Shanghai for delivery in August. However, according to some investigations, this matter is still unclear. Checking the August futures market accounts, there were no extremely large sellers. Moreover, the prices are not very cost-effective. However, a certain short position in the distant months continued to increase its holdings. As for the Rongxinghao long position, it continued to buy in the near month. The long and short sides are fighting fiercely. In general, the price of 50 taels is likely to fluctuate greatly at some point. However, the situation of the Rehe military is still serious, and the snowstorm is spreading, which has a significant impact.

The recent drop in yarn reached two to three taels. Before the market opened, American cotton was flat, and rumors in the mid-session that a large amount of Tianjin yarn would be delivered in August caused a sharp drop of one tael. In the second and third sessions, the price fell by seven or eight qian, and the situation weakened further. All months broke the 50-tael mark. As a result, all months fell by one tael and seven or eight qian to three taels and two qian. The total volume of transactions was 46,550 bales. Last Week, American Cotton Followed Wheat and Securities to Firmness 147

New York, 29th telegraphs the cotton market conditions for the week: In the past week, there have been showers in the central and eastern cotton belts, causing fears of bollworm damage. In addition, the wheat and securities markets have been strong, and the business community is optimistic. As a result, raw cotton prices have suddenly rebounded. Trading on the cotton exchange has been relatively light at times, but trading has become more active when prices rise. Local and bank streets have made considerable additions. It is believed that representatives of the Bureau of Agriculture are still continuing to sell, with approximately 10,000 bales of October futures being sold daily. It is also heard here that Southern Cooperatives have sold spot cotton, and the amount of cotton sold to Europe and the Far East is quite large. The price will be settled after August 1, when the new cotton season begins. The method by which the Bureau of Agriculture will promote its inventory of 650,000 bales of cotton in the next season has not yet been determined, so buyers are afraid to buy in easily. 38 Shi of New Early Rice Arrived Yesterday 149

Yesterday, at more than ten rice shops on Rice Market West Road in South Shanghai, North Japonica rice was extremely difficult to sell, and the price fell by two jiao. Jiangsu and Tongbei Japonica rice also tended to decline. The decline in early and late indica rice from Qingjiao and Sisong became more prevalent, falling by about two jiao, due to sluggish buying interest. New goods were launched, and production areas reported softness. In the afternoon, another 38 shi of new Japonica rice arrived, and prices opened with a sharp drop of 5 jiao to 1 yuan.

Yesterday, about thirteen or fourteen boats arrived in North Shanghai. Trading on this street was not good. Changshu and Wuxi North Japonica rice were softer by one jiao, and the next smaller by two or three jiao. Early and late indica rice from the villages remained unchanged. The opening price in the morning was lower by one or two jiao, and the sales of cooked rice were also weak. The situation was declining. Although the arrival of Luyang pointed rice was rare, there was no change.

The new Japonica rice was similar to that in South Shanghai.

Foreign Rice Prices Drop and Sales Pick Up 150

Saigon Rice Drops to Within Ten Yuan

Yesterday, the foreign rice market initially appeared soft and tired due to weak sales in recent days. Some cargo owners were eager to sell, so market prices recovered slightly. Subsequently, mainland buyers, seeing the market price recover slightly, planned to ship goods and bought more than 3,000 bags of new and old small-sized rice. Zhenjiang, Jiangbei, and villages on this street all made inquiries, and the market showed signs of activity, with prices also recovering. The market opened with 3,000 bags of small-sized rice, priced at 9.35 to 9.2 yuan, and 4,000 bags of old small-sized rice, priced at 9.1 to 8.8 yuan. In addition, 200 bags of Saigon rice were priced at only 9.95 yuan.

Sparse July Flour Delivery Volume 151

Yesterday was the delivery day for July flour. The total delivery volume throughout the day was very light. Only Huafeng delivered 7,000 bags of green wheat root flour, which was taken away by this street. The remaining factories had all purchased in advance on their own, so there were no deliveries. Currently, the sales of spot flour are active due to the upcoming Mid-Autumn Festival mooncake season. Sales in various ports, both domestic and foreign, are lively. In addition, wheat prices have recently shown a declining trend, so the market for out-of-month flour is expected to remain strong.

New Xu Kui Sunflower Seeds Open at 16 Taels 152

The first batch of new black sunflower seeds, mostly Xu Kui seeds, arrived in the past two days and immediately opened at a price of 16 taels. As more batches arrive, the price will inevitably loosen. It is found that each shop still has old inventory. The current selling price for top-grade seeds is 16 taels, followed by 14 taels or so, and then 11 taels or so. The trend is stable.

Sugar Market: Raw and Red Sugar Tend to Rise 153

Coarse Sugar and White Sugar Market Stabilizes

Yesterday, the Sugar Market Association held its market session. Due to relatively flat sentiment and the fact that it was Saturday, transactions were very sparse. Brisk Trade in Green Tea 156
