Water Bills Can Be Reduced Appropriately 188

The Public Works Department Information Office announced that at the Public Works Department Board meeting, the General Manager reported that after the Water Company changed to a meter system, some places increased significantly compared to the previous lump-sum system. This matter is currently under investigation. It is proposed to ask the Board to allow water charges to be reduced during this period, but the condition is that the total income should not be reduced and the water rate table does not need to be increased. The General Manager reported at the meeting that the Water Company found that water consumption has greatly increased recently during the hot summer, so the owners of a large number of houses may have to pay a lot more according to the meter system. The company intends to ask for permission to give appropriate reductions in case of such difficulties. The General Manager's intention is that this proposal is a temporary measure. If it does not cause an increase in the water rate table, it seems permissible. After discussion, the directors resolved: 1. If no demands for compensation are made to the Public Works Department, 2. The company shall report the details of each household whose fees have been reduced each month, as well as the impact of the meter system on water consumption and the company's income. Then, the request for temporary permission to reduce fees can be approved.

Citizens' Association Representatives 189

Requesting the Cancellation of Telephone Rate Increase

Reasons Presented to the Public Works Department Yesterday

The Special Committee Against Telephone Rate Increase of the Citizens' Association decided at its second committee meeting to appoint Chen Binghui, Zhou Fuzhang, Zhang Xianfang, Zhuang Zhihe, and others to petition the Public Works Department to instruct the Telephone Company to cancel the rate increase. The representatives went to the Public Works Department at 10:00 AM yesterday. General Manager Johns of the Public Works Department was out, and He Dekui, the Associate General Manager, received them. The representatives stated four reasons: (1) According to the telephone company's notice of rate increase in the concession, this increase is due to the installation of automatic switchboards, but cities such as Hong Kong and Nanjing have also installed automatic switchboards without raising rates. (2) The association's petition to cancel the rate increase is based on the public opinion of the 3 million citizens in the Special District, as the association has been receiving letters from more than 6,000 users opposing the rate increase. (3) After the company installed the automatic switchboards, it laid off a large number of operators, so the expenses have been saved and are sufficient to compensate for the losses of the installation. (4) The association should ask your bureau to seriously note that the company must not take any action such as cutting off lines or removing machines before the association's negotiations are resolved. After the representatives finished speaking, Mr. He said that the company's rate increase this time is based on the proposal of the telephone expert An Sheng in 1929. Because An Sheng suggested to the company at that time that it should allocate 8 million yuan of capital from 1929 to 1932 for the installation of automatic switchboards. The capital has been fully used up by March of this year, so it is necessary to increase the rate for users by 25% to compensate. Your bureau has promised An Sheng's proposal in the past, and the company has gradually done so according to An Sheng's method, so the rate increase proposal should be approved. However, now that telephone users have risen up in opposition, I will accept your representatives' opinions and forward them to the General Manager for consideration. At the same time, I hope that your association can organize a joint association of users to negotiate with the company in a reasonable manner. The representatives then left. The association is now scheduled to hold the third special committee meeting against telephone rate increase at the association at 2:00 PM on August

2nd (Tuesday) to report on the negotiations with the Public Works Department and discuss future plans.

Gaogiao Seaside Bathing Beach Free for Swimming 190

The municipal authorities have recently arranged a seaside bathing beach on the east beach of Gaogiao Town, Pudong. In addition to building houses for tourists to change clothes, rest, or dine, they have also planted cloth umbrellas all over the beach and set up cloth chairs for bathers to rest. Water rulers have also been erected in the water to ensure that bathers know the depth and location to avoid danger. It is heard that some people in the public are wondering if there will be a charge for swimming there. Someone went to inquire yesterday and was told that the purpose of setting up the bathing beach this time is to use the city's only natural beach, add some equipment, and provide it for citizens to enjoy. This is a necessary facility in the city, so in addition to charging fees for using the changing rooms to make up for the expenses, swimming is free of charge and there is no so-called admission ticket.

Gongguan Road 191

French Newspaper Robbed

Two Thieves Robbed Over 2,000 Yuan

Thieves Fired Three Shots at Police, Fortunately Missing

The French newspaper at 23 Gongguan Road, French Concession, is the only French newspaper in this city. It has been established for many years and employs many workers. Yesterday happened to be the end of the solar month, which was the date for paying wages. Somehow, it was detected by thieves. At about 11:00 AM yesterday, two thieves, one wearing white silk shirt and trousers and the other wearing light blue shorts and speaking in local accents, suddenly came. One of the thieves wearing white silk held a pistol and broke in through the gate, invaded the second floor, went straight into the accounting room, raised the gun to scare and forbid screaming. They robbed more than 2,000 yuan of newly deposited wages in the iron box and carried it to escape. The gatekeeper, Constable Wang Chengji (from Anhui, 33 years old), heard the alarm and went out to chase, but was turned back by the thief, who fired three shots at the constable. Fortunately, the constable dodged quickly, so all three shots missed. The thieves then took the opportunity to escape without a trace. Afterwards, the newspaper filed a report with the police station, requesting them to pursue the thieves.

Robbery in West Shanghai 192

Three Houses Robbed in One Night

The house of the late farmer Xu Baoquan in Yujiatang North House, south of Hongqiao Town in West Shanghai, was well-to-do and had recently been coveted by robbers. At about 11:00 PM the night before last (29th), eight or nine robbers who spoke in mixed accents suddenly broke into the house. The whole Xu family was awakened from their dreams. The robbers used ropes to tie the hands of the whole family behind their backs and threatened them with guns. Then, they turned boxes and cabinets upside down and searched arbitrarily, robbing clothes and ornaments worth about four or five hundred yuan. After about an hour, they all roared and went south. After robbing, the robbers went to the houses of two farmers, Qin Dianqing and Qin Fugeng, in Qinjiabiao, about three miles south of Yujiatang. It was heard that Qin's daughter would be married in September, so all the clothes and ornaments prepared for the wedding were robbed. The victims have now issued a list of losses and reported it to the police station in charge, requesting them to solve the case within a limited time to maintain peace in the area.

Female Worker and Western Servant Living Together 193

Western Servant Sentenced to Six Months in Prison

Female Worker Taken Back by Her Father

Sun Afeng, a woman from Ningbo, was 29 years old, petite and exquisite, with a dark complexion, living at 49 1/2 Oujia Road. She worked as a cigarette roller at the Huaping Tobacco Company on Huade Road. The company faced a Westerner's residence, which employed Yuan Yehai, a servant from Tianjin, who was 23 years old. When the woman got off work, he seduced her in every way and they became intimate with each other. On May 8th, he lured Sun to his house at 183 Tuoga Road and lived together as if they were husband and wife. Her father, Sun Songlai, searched everywhere for his daughter after she disappeared, but there was no news and he was troubled all day long. There was no trace to be found. The afternoon before yesterday, he was strolling idly on Tuogao Road when he saw his daughter Afeng playing on the road. Sun Songlai remained calm and secretly followed her. He saw the woman enter the house at 183, and then he knew that she had been lured and hidden there to live together. So he secretly reported to the Jiaxing Road Police Station. The head of the police, Liu Zhongcheng, and a Western detective went to arrest Yuan Yehai and took the woman Sun Afeng to the police station together. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Fourth Criminal Court of the First Special District. The police station's lawyer, Zhang Tianyin, stated the previous situation and requested an investigation. Then, Sun Songlai, the woman's father, reported the situation and said that he had gone to other places when his daughter disappeared, and he only found out about it when he returned. The court ordered Sun Afeng to stand in the witness box for questioning. The woman was dressed in modern fashion with a bobbed hairstyle, wearing a pink floral chiffon cheongsam, silk stockings, and satin shoes. She was not shy at all and said calmly that she was 18 years old, did not know her birthday, and was a female worker at the Huaping Cigarette Factory on Huade Road. The defendant was a servant in the Westerner's house opposite the factory. I fell in love with him. During the war in Shanghai, it had been five months. Before, I went home to tell my mother and tried to get her consent, but I was scolded by my mother, so I had to go out and rent a room with the defendant on Tuogao Road and was willing to marry him as his wife. When questioned, the defendant confessed that he had fallen in love with Sun Afeng, and it was the woman's own will. Before, he asked her to go home and inform her mother to formally marry him, but he did not get what he wanted. He gave ambiguous answers and asked for judgment. Judge Fu Lin verified the confession and declared to both parties that although modern trends are not ancient, marriage matters should seek the consent of parents and should not be perfunctory, thinking that it is voluntary. Therefore, Yuan Yehai was sentenced to six months of imprisonment as a warning, and the woman Sun Afeng was taken back by her father Sun Songlai for discipline. When the woman heard the sentence, she did not want to go home and was willing to eat official lawsuits with the defendant. Judge Fu earnestly instructed the woman and also told her father not to abuse her. Afeng then bowed her head and followed her father home.

Wife's Excuse of Returning to Ningbo 194

Actually Cohabiting with a Paramour

Su Kaisheng, a Yancheng native residing at 519 Youheng Road East, through the matchmaking of Li Bigu in the 18th year [of the Republic, i.e., 1929], married Yin Di, the daughter of Xu Shanggui and Xu Sun, residing at 945 Yuanfang Lane, Old Huaihai Road East. Unexpectedly, after the marriage, Yin Di yearned for her mother's home and frequently returned to Ningbo. Su repeatedly tried to stop her, but Yin Di not only disregarded his warnings but also incited the anger of her parents, causing the relationship between father-in-law and son-in-law to deteriorate daily. On the eighth of this month, Yin Di again returned home without notice. By dusk the next day, she still had not returned, so Su went to visit her parents' home. Her parents claimed that she had not gone there, arousing great suspicion. He rushed home to check the luggage, only to find that all the clothes inside had been taken. He then discovered that Yin Di had an affair with Hu Guibao, residing at 120 Yuanchang Road, and used the excuse of returning to Ningbo to secretly meet with Hu. Her parents were fully aware of this but did not restrain her, and this had been going on for a long time. Su, understanding the whole situation, concluded that Xu Shanggui and others were colluding with each other. Besides reporting to the police and requesting an investigation, he also filed a criminal self-accusation against Xu and his wife, as well as Hu Guibao, with the First Special District Local Court, accusing them of adultery, absconding with property, and instigation. Judge Wu held a court hearing yesterday, summoned the parties for questioning, and announced that the trial would be rescheduled.

Part of the Robbers Arrested 195

Jiutai Cigarette and Paper Store Case 196

One Fugitive, Three Arrested

The Jiutai Cigarette and Paper Store at 102 Hengxing East Lane, Waima Road outside the Sixteenth Bund in the South City, was robbed of approximately two thousand yuan worth of goods on June 29th of this year. Dong Mingde, the section leader of the First District of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, recently received a tip that the robbers Zhu Yaoting and Shen Guisheng were hiding at 77 Peide Lane, Xinzha Road in northern Shanghai. He immediately led detectives Yuan Haishan, Yu Maolong, Peng Baolin, and others to the address the day before yesterday. Upon learning of their arrival, Shen Guisheng immediately escaped by climbing over the window onto the roof. When Dong and the others went upstairs, Shen was nowhere to be found. They arrested Shen's concubine, Zhang Li (nicknamed "Needle Girl"), and Zhu Yaoting's wife, Zhu Lin. They also found a pistol and thirty-one bullets in the toilet in the room and took them away. They also found a fake pistol in the garbage can in the lane. Just as they were about to take it back, Zhu Yaoting returned from outside. Seeing the detectives, he immediately fled, but Dong and the others caught him at the intersection of Shanhaiguan Road, took him back for preliminary interrogation. Zhu Yaoting confessed that he was twenty-eight years old, from Tongzhou, and had come to Shanghai with his wife, Zhu Lin, this spring. He had met his old friend Shen Guisheng and moved in with him at 77 Peide Lane. Shen used to work at the Longmao Fruit Store on the Sixteenth Bund but was now unemployed and financially strapped. On June 28th, he gathered Zhu, Gu Laoqi, A He, and the Monk, and the four of them met in front of the Hongzhang Yarn Factory west of Sanban Bridge in the North City. They agreed to rob the Jiutai Cigarette and Paper Store at around 6:00 AM the next morning. The stolen goods had already been divided and spent. Zhu Lin confessed that she was twenty-one years old, from Tongzhou, and Zhu Yaoting was her husband. When the detectives came to arrest them, Shen Guisheng told her to hide the pistol and thirty-one bullets in the toilet before escaping through the window. As for her husband's robbery of Jiutai, she knew nothing about it. Zhang Li confessed that she was twenty-two years old, from Tongzhou. Her former paramour was named Li Zhicheng, but after he was arrested for robbery, she had no choice but to become involved with Shen Guisheng, not expecting him to be a thief as well, leading to her implication. Gu A Xiang, who had fled with Zhu, confessed that he was twenty-five years old, from Wuxi, and worked as a tailor at 15 Sande Lane, Baker Road. The day before yesterday, he had gone to Peide Lane to visit a friend but had not found him, so he was waiting at the entrance of the lane when he suddenly saw detectives arresting robbers. Fearing danger, he had fled in a panic. The case was deemed important because it involved robbery, and they were ordered to prepare a document and send it to the bureau for further investigation.

Tragic Fall from Scaffolding Resulting in Death 197

Song Heshang, a thirty-four-year-old Shaoxing native, opened the Hexing Western Clothing Store at 930 Wuchang Road. Yesterday afternoon at around 5:00 PM, he and his colleagues were installing the glass for the awning on the third floor. Due to the excessive weight, the wooden frame could not support it, and he lost his footing and fell, breaking his leg bones and causing severe bleeding from his abdomen. His wife rushed him to the Tongren Hospital, but treatment was ineffective. He died at 8:30 PM. The hospital moved the body to the coroner's office, awaiting notification of the court for examination.

Dr. Liu Wu-chi Returns to China Today 198

Dr. Liu Wu-chi is the brilliant and handsome son of Central Supervisory Committee member Mr. Liu Yazi. In the 16th year of the Republic [i.e., 1927], he graduated from Tsinghua University with outstanding grades. He then went to study in the United States, entering Lawrence University and graduating in the 17th year [i.e., 1928]. He then transferred to the Yale University Graduate School, specializing in English literature, and graduated in the 20th year [i.e., 1931], earning a Ph.D. in literature. Mr. Liu is learned and eloquent, excelling in both Chinese and Western literature. His works, such as "Chronicle of Su Manshu" and "Young Goethe" ("Bodhi Beads"), have long been praised by readers. His occasional writings, scattered in Chinese and foreign newspapers and magazines, are also of high quality. Last autumn, he left the United States for a tour of Europe. The month before last, he married his beloved, Miss Gao Hong (who graduated from Meng Hua Li Women's University and studied public health and microbiology at the Yale University Graduate School), at the Chinese Consulate in London, England. It is said that he has already set off from Europe to return to China on the Italian mail ship Conte Rosso, which is expected to arrive at the northern wharf of the China Merchants Bureau in Hongkou at 1:00 PM today.

Weather Report 212

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday said that the Shandong coast is clear with a strong southeasterly wind. The Yangtze River basin and the coast south of Ma'an Island are mostly cloudy with strong southeasterly winds and occasional showers. The southern East China Sea and the area around Taiwan have bad weather, with strong cyclones. This is because a cyclone on the Pacific Ocean is east of the Balingtang Strait, moving northwest or west-northwest. The center of the cyclone was about 120 miles within the intersection of 26 degrees north latitude and 122 degrees east longitude at about 6:00 AM, gradually weakening. One was about 60 miles within the intersection of 21 degrees north latitude and 126 degrees east longitude at about 2:00 PM, but the wind force is unknown. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the temperature in this city was a maximum of 93.9 and a minimum of 78.8. On the same day last year, the maximum was 91.8 and the minimum was 75.9.

Shenbao Local Supplement

Comments

Restricting Public Servants from Criticizing Government Facilities 219

— Buddha

I most welcome people scolding [me]. If the scolding is correct, I can learn from it and improve. If the scolding is incorrect, it is like a rooster crowing or a dog barking. They lose their own character and can be ignored. That is my opinion.

According to yesterday's news, the National Government has ordered all agencies that, in the future, if public servants believe that government facilities are inappropriate, they can submit written suggestions to their superiors and must not publish them to the outside world on their own. Those who violate this will be subject to disciplinary action by the competent superiors, depending on the circumstances. This is correct, because since they are public servants, if they believe that the government's measures are inappropriate, they can suggest them to the competent superiors, asking them to adopt them, or asking them to submit them to the authorities for consideration and adoption. It is not necessary to publish opinions to the outside world on one's own initiative. However, non-public servants, if they believe that the government's measures are inappropriate, do not seem to need to use the suggestion procedure and can freely publish them to the outside world. This sentence is implied, and it is self-evident. However, the government allows the people to freely express their opinions, which is originally the principle of the people's freedom of speech. Naturally, in freedom of speech, there are those who speak correctly and those who speak incorrectly. This is entirely up to the government's will. If the government believes that what is said is correct, it can adopt it as much as possible. If it believes that it is incorrect, it can be placed under the example of not discussing or discussing it. This is seeing the government's bright and upright attitude.

Preventing the people's mouths is worse than preventing rivers. As the ancient saying goes, it is even worse now. Moreover, from ancient times to the present, the government's means of preventing mouths can be said to have been exhausted. May I ask which dynasty or generation has had an effect? There is also another layer, preventing mouths is easy, preventing hearts is even more difficult. Although the mouth does not speak, the heart actually opposes. How can it be prevented? There is also another layer, if one openly and freely expresses opinions, they are a straightforward person. Although their words may be foolish, their hearts have no other intentions. For example, when encountering a dog, if it sees a person, it will bark loudly and firmly. That dog is definitely not fierce. What is most frightening is that there is no indication at first. Once you get close, it will jump out and bite wildly. This is really terrible.

It is said that only good people can accept exhaustive words. It is not easy to accept exhaustive words. Without a selfless attitude and a humble mind, when one hears unpleasant words, one cannot help but (anger rises from the heart and evil grows from the gallbladder). Therefore, the ancients said that only good people can accept exhaustive words.

Science

Lightning Rod 222

— Yin Zhen

(1) The installation of a lightning rod is very simple. A sharp metal pillar is installed on the roof, connected with thick copper wires, and a copper plate is buried in a damp place underground. This copper plate is connected to the thick copper wires. This installation is the installation of a lightning rod.

(2) The reason why lightning rods prevent lightning is that during thunderstorms, the induced electricity generated on the ground is slowly dissipated into the air by the sharp end, so the house is not subject to severe electrical shocks.

(3) The principle of lightning rod application The distribution of electricity is limited to the surface of conductors (metal-like objects that cause the easy movement of electrodes), and the curved places have more electricity than the flat places. Therefore, the sharper the column, the more electricity it carries. Because the sharp end has a large amount of electricity, the substances around the column are first attracted and finally repelled. (1) Therefore, all the electricity of the charged body is gradually lost, which is called the tip effect. The lightning rod is a kind of safety device made by applying the principle of the tip effect. (1) It is the property of electricity that the same sex repels each other and the opposite sex attracts each other.

(4) The effect of lightning rods After the lightning rod is installed on the house, whenever there is a thunderstorm, when the electric light and thunder are very intense, the nearby houses, people and animals will be struck by lightning. The family with the lightning rod installed can avoid this danger, so the lightning rod is also a part of the safety device. Now it is summer, and this kind of thing is just right, so I contribute it to you.

Suggestions for Improving the Kitchen in the Social Improvement Discussion 223

— Holding Buddha

The kitchen of a family is the most important part, but Shanghai people don't pay much attention to it. The living room and bedroom are very particular, with luxurious and splendid furnishings, but the kitchen is only controlled by servants, and it is unbearably dirty. It is really a strange thing. If you go to the major mansions in Shanghai for investigation, you will definitely be shocked.

Originally, the masters, wives, young ladies, and grandmothers in the mansions would reach out for tea and open their mouths for food. They would not condescend to manage the affairs in the kitchen. They left it to the servants and let them be hygienic or unhygienic. They didn't know that the kitchen is where the food and drink come from, which is of great importance to health and disease. Especially in autumn and summer, it is common to see food not covered, flies flying on it, and leftovers cold and scorched, tilting east and flowing west, which is unbearably dirty. Isn't this the most unhygienic? The masters, wives, young ladies, and grandmothers only know that the rice is fragrant and the dishes are fresh, but they don't know that the food contains many germs.

In ordinary families, a kitchen is shared by four or five families. One rice basket east and one bamboo cabinet west, vegetables, fish, rice, and meat are scattered all over the floor, and the stench is pungent, which is disgusting. The most unhygienic thing is that the toilet is often outside the kitchen. Often, next to the tap water pipe, rice is washed and vegetables are washed. Thinking carefully, isn't it dirty, isn't it harmful? In restaurants on the sea, the toilet is often very close to the place where wine is heated, which is really nauseating. In the interior, the firewood room and the pit latrine are often adjacent to the kitchen, which is easy to catch fire and easy to spread germs. These things may seem like small things at first glance, but they are actually very important. Therefore, I put forward this suggestion for improving the kitchen.

Suggestions on Children's Toys 224

— Yi Nong

The personality of our youth is developed in childhood, and the personality of children is closely related to their toys. Most ignorant men and women in our country use toys such as insects, fish, birds and beasts, and foreign dolls to feed their children. This kind of toy is a waste of money and has no benefit to the children's body and mind. Moreover, the source of this kind of toy is mostly from our country's arch-enemy, Japan!

I have seen Western children, except for very young girls, never play with toys such as foreign dolls. What they play with are small knives, axes, and small engines made in their own country. They use these toys to make various small toys themselves. This spirit is truly amazing.

Wooden knives, guns, swords, and halberds are purely national quintessence toys in our country. This kind of toy must be criticized by general modern people as barbaric. In fact, using this to feed children can best cultivate their martial spirit, which can just eliminate the sluggishness of our people.

As for the well-to-do families, they can buy Western-made toys, such as small air guns and small engines, to feed their children. This kind of toy can make children's minds more scientific, so that they will become scientific and useful youth in the future.

I have two young brothers, and the toys I have given them over the years are only a few wooden knives and two cheap small air guns. I used these toys to teach them the preliminary national art and shallow military knowledge. I dare not be confident that this is a good idea, but at least it is not as unprofitable as playing with all unconscious toys!

In short, the choice of toys greatly affects the future of children. Now I would like to make this suggestion, and I hope that all colleagues in this association will discuss it.

A Corner of Society

An Account of a Strange Affair 225

— Wu

Friend, have you been to the North Railway Station? Then have you paid attention to everything there? If not, I will tell you about a strange affair. Haha, it is truly a strange affair unique to our esteemed China. ··Oh? You don't believe it? Just wait and listen to me explain in detail.

Friend! The North Station was burned to ruins by the enemy, but apart from the railway police, there is still a large armed police force (maintaining order), just like before the war. They are both imposing and dignified!

It was still early, and an old man with tattered clothes carrying a load hurried up. Because the train was about to depart, he was naturally in a hurry; but he was stopped by the police's roar. Then, the tightly tied rope

Page 18

Shen Bao Local Supplement

was untied. Under the so-called (inspection) procedure, the old man's belongings were thrown one by one on the ground. They rummaged and rummaged, inspected and inspected again. Although the old man repeatedly begged for forgiveness because the train was about to depart, he waited until the train had left but the inspection was still not finished.

Then what happened afterwards? Haha, friend! That was truly interesting. Although these police officers didn't find any contraband, one of them took two bread rolls worth one hundred cash, smelled them near his nose, and then impolitely put them in his mouth and chewed. Ugh! Friend! What do you think this behavior is? It's simply highway robbery!

Of course, the robbed person could only stare blankly and remain speechless. However, friend! This is precisely the achievement of our esteemed country in maintaining law and order!

Such a Principal 226

After the former principal of X School ascended to heaven, the foreigners spent three whole months with great difficulty inviting a Doctor to serve as the principal. The principal was just a symbolic figurehead. For the Doctor to come and head the school, given his degree, it seemed a pity to make him a lackey-like principal of a middle school. However, perhaps he wouldn't be like the deceased scholar-principal. Perhaps he had the determination to run education and would earnestly reform the Church school. This was the speculation of us students before he took office.

When he took office, he met with the graduating class. At that time, we, the hundreds of students, eagerly inquired about his opinion on the problem of official registration, which we were looking forward to, and requested him to resolve it quickly. If the Municipal Education Bureau seriously does its job and closes down unregistered schools, then the registration problem will not be difficult to solve.) Um, the purpose of his being the principal was not to improve the school, but to hope for the downfall of X School; not to enlighten the stubborn Western priests, but to obey them. This was the initial impression he gave us.

After he took office, X School saw a new figure: someone in a Western suit, carrying a briefcase, running around busily. In terms of school administration, apart from deliberately suspending a dean of studies and hiring a gentleman with the same surname from the principal's hometown to serve as dean of studies, he also dragged a group of fellow villagers to fill teaching positions. Perhaps the Doctor thought he was being underutilized, so much so that he neglected the national salvation movement, or even the September 18th Incident. This Doctor, who specialized in obeying foreigners, caused a

shutdown farce because of his neglect of duty.

However, his good points should also be praised. He shouldn't be abruptly dismissed. He was particularly enthusiastic about religious affairs and was greatly praised by the Western priests. Therefore, after X School closed down, he honorably became a staff member of the Church bookstore. (But reward)

Road to 227

Death 228

— Bai Hong

My friend, Mr. T, has been unemployed for more than half a year. He only buys some sesame flatbread and fried dough sticks to fill his stomach every day. Sometimes, he doesn't even have the money to buy sesame flatbread and fried dough sticks, so he simply sleeps and doesn't eat. He thinks about it day after day, always hoping that when the situation is peaceful, he can immediately find a

position to make a living. But ah, reality tells him there is no hope. Recently, even Mr. A, who helped him survive, has lost his job!

The day before yesterday, they wrote a letter saying that they had not had food for three or four days and wanted to ask Mr. B for help. But Mr. B himself had reached the end of his rope. After receiving the letter, he sighed deeply and sat there in silent thought.

In this year of terrible hunger, unfortunately, Mr. A fell ill. It is said that the illness is very serious and there is no hope. Naturally, being so poor that they can't even afford food, where can they afford to hire a doctor? They can only let him die.

That group of people who have not died but are tormented by poverty are constantly threatened by death. Recently, the number of unemployed people is increasing, and those who are not unemployed have reached the era of bankruptcy. In short, everyone is walking on the road to death. Who created this! (This is entirely the terrifying era created by the policy of non-resistance!) Mr. T said angrily in a letter one day, (If we were asked to go to the front line to fight, then we would have no regrets even if we died, but to starve us to death alive, we will not rest in peace even in death!)

Isn't that so? Now the customs duties have been looted, the post office has been looted, Rehe is in danger, and Tianjin and Beiping are shaking. Everything is in a mess. The country has already reached the point of bankruptcy, let alone the common people. If things continue like this, the various countries don't need to send a single soldier, and they don't need any dum-dum bullets, smoke bombs, battleships, or airplanes. They only need to send a few well-dressed civil officials to jointly manage China's finances, and China will be finished. Japan's dispatch of troops seems unnecessary.

However, in this year of peril and ruin, the majority of the people still live their lives with equanimity. Young people still go to movie theaters, dance halls, and engage in romance. The ignorant masses, although they are walking on the road to death, only sigh a few times about their own misfortune. Chinese people treat other Chinese people, and if they disagree, they will treat each other with their fists. But when they are slapped by a foreigner, not only do they not retaliate, but they also respectfully offer a smile.

Alas! This era is full of signs of walking on the road to national demise. Road to death!

Jinbao 229

— Kang Shi

Every time Auntie Si returned to the countryside from Shanghai, she wore a new-style cheongsam, her hair was neatly and smoothly cut, her exquisite watch, and her sparkling gold earrings were especially worthy of people's attention!

Everyone envied her for having such happiness and beauty as a maid in Shanghai!

Jinbao was the most enthusiastic admirer, and she often dreamed of her ideal dream at night.

She asked her parents many times, (I want to go to Shanghai with Auntie Si to work as a maid.) But her parents always refused and advised her, (You are so young, what do you know? Shanghai is a den of all kinds of evil, it's better not to go!) But vanity gnawed in people's hearts, and the power of magic was so great that she came up with a plan.

(Auntie Si! I want to go to Shanghai with you to work as a maid, but my parents won't allow it. Please recommend me to my parents!) Jinbao said to her when Auntie Si was in the countryside.

Indeed, Jinbao's parents heard that Auntie Si was recommending their daughter and would do her best to take care of her. Money is loved by everyone, so Jinbao's parents agreed to Jinbao going to Shanghai with Auntie Si to work as a maid!

Jinbao has been working as a maid in a brothel in Shanghai for three years. Her parents, because her wedding date was approaching, had repeatedly asked Auntie Si to urge her to go back. But she had already found a lover in the environment of desire, so she repeatedly made excuses and refused to go back. How would her parents know that!

Because her wedding date was imminent, her father had no choice but to go to Shanghai to find her. He saw that she was no longer the her from the countryside three years ago. She was wearing a fashionable cheongsam, and her braids were gone. Her high-heeled leather shoes were polished so brightly that they reflected people, and she had become a modern woman. Of course, in the process of women's transformation, one can see their integrity. Jinbao was also one of the transformed. How shocked her father was! He forced her to return quickly.

A week after Jinbao's wedding, she disappeared.

(Jinbao's mother! Didn't Auntie Si go to find Jinbao yesterday? This must be Auntie Si's trick. Several similar things in the village must have been done by her. She specializes in luring women from the countryside to satisfy her desire for wealth. Alas! Detestable Auntie Si! You shouldn't have deceived my beloved Jinbao····) Jinbao's father said with tears····

The Entanglements of Grandfather and Grandson's Correspondence 230

— Lin Xia

Yongxin is a very smart and literary young man. He is only seventeen years old and has already graduated from high school. This time he came to Shanghai with me to take the university entrance exam. In his spare time, he only studies and reads newspapers at home. In less than half a month, he has already remembered many novel phrases from the new literature.

Recently, he respectfully sent a letter to his grandfather:

(Respectfully reporting to Grandfather's knees: The universities in Shanghai are really a mess. The day before yesterday, Mr. Zhang told me (the male and female students of Shanghai K University only know how to pursue modernization every day. They don't attend classes. Either they find a mister to have a good time, or they borrow a pass from Miss Wang's black bench to go to the French Park for fun, or they gather a group of comrades to go swimming at the beach, and have picnics in the wild, playing happily. They only open their books when they have to, and they complain bitterly after reading half a page. When it comes to major exams, fortunately they have many friends and can obtain passes. They still answer the questions fully, and the teachers are lenient and give everyone a pass. ) A university like this is really misleading young people. Your grandson will definitely not take its exam,···)

His grandfather was so angry when he received this letter that his beard stood on end. He read it dozens of times, wondering if his grandson was talking nonsense or spouting nonsense. He picked up a pen and wrote a strongly reprimanding handwritten instruction····

(···Reading your report, it is full of glib talk and I don't know what it means. Have you caught the epidemic and are talking nonsense? Does modernization produce dogs or rats? The black bench is a seating tool. What is there to borrow? And what kind of monster is a pass? What is even stranger is that the same word "pass" is used three times, but the meanings cannot be combined. The meaning of "place and occasion" in your report seems to be (time) (moment). Why not use the original word directly and replace it with "place and occasion"? You are young, so I will forgive you once. If you continue to make such a fuss and fill the page with nonsense, I will definitely not forgive you···)

Yongxin realized after receiving his grandfather's stern letter that his grandfather had not studied English or Japanese. No wonder he regarded these phrases as complete nonsense. He found it funny instead.

I think this kind of joke is probably not just happening to my fellow villager!

Why

The Unfaithful Lover 231

— Qiu Lang

He has been in Shanghai from the countryside for only five years in total, I believe. This is something I witnessed with my own eyes. In the beginning, there was a kind of rustic demeanor that can still be reflected in my mind.

He was an ordinary staff member in XX store. His salary was naturally limited. He liked to eat some snacks, and each month, after deducting all expenses, he had a little surplus to save. In the winter of the second year, his family made the decision for him to marry a village girl as his wife. At that time, I also sent a small gift. As for him? He naturally returned to his hometown with joy to be a bridegroom!

When he came back after his marriage, I and several of his colleagues swarmed around him, wanting him to announce the process of his marriage and report to the public. Although he didn't say a word, the expression on his face of raised eyebrows and constant smiles was enough to represent the joy in his heart! The sweetness of love!

One year 丨 two years 丨 three years, time flies forward non-stop. Strangely enough! All of his actions were also rapidly changing and progressing. From the top of his head to the heels of his feet, he dressed up beautifully! Not only did he not dare to be considered a country person anymore, but everyone was probably calling him a big spender! At the same time, when he saw these modern girls in Shanghai, how could he not feel lively in his heart! Occasionally, when he thought of the yellow-faced village wife at home, he couldn't help but feel puzzled, annoyed, and resentful. As a result, he had long harbored the thought in the depths of his heart! Village girl! You cannot grow old with me!

The poor woman: she couldn't even dream that she had been abandoned by her husband! Every day she still carries out her housework step by step. But as the days went by, she never received a letter from her husband, and no money was sent home. She was suspicious, anxious, and finally resolutely decided to come to Shanghai and stayed in XX Hotel, calling the tea server to ask her husband to come to XX store.

He had no choice but to rush to XX Hotel to meet her. The moment he saw her, he cursed, (What are you doing here? Are you here to die!) She naturally (shed tears before speaking), and later, I don't know how he incited his anger and was viciously beaten by him, running away angrily and no one knew where!

Alas! Prosperous Shanghai, filthy Shanghai! I don't know to what extent you will lure people! And how much evil will you create!

Shanghai Second Special District Local Court 235

▲ Civil Judgments: Zhang Hanshen vs. Jin Zhongying for payment of rent and return of property: The defendant should pay the plaintiff 350 taels of silver in rent; the remainder of the plaintiff's claim is rejected; one-fifth of the litigation costs borne by the plaintiff, four-fifths borne by the defendant. ▲ Zhou Qiaosun vs. Wang Fucheng et al. for payment of rent: Defendant Wang Fucheng, Zhang Afu, and Xu Fengxiang should each pay the plaintiff 57 yuan and 2 jiao in rent; Defendant Shen Sanbao should pay the plaintiff 66 yuan in rent and return the property located at No. 35 Yongde Li, Lanwei Ai Road, leased to him; the remainder of the plaintiff's claim is rejected; litigation costs to be borne by the defendants proportionally; this judgment concerning the return of the leased property will be provisionally executed. ▲ Yuanyuan Silver Company vs. Ren Pu Tian Le for rent arrears: The defendant should pay the plaintiff 720 taels of silver in rent; the remainder of the plaintiff's claim is rejected; litigation costs borne by the defendant. ▲ Sanglutong Tianjin Apartment vs. Lin Changheng for compensation: Appeal dismissed; costs of the second instance borne by the appellant. ▲ Tang Wenbin vs. Zhang Zhiming et al. for debt: Defendants Zhang Zhiming, Jiang Hengchang, and Pan Dasheng should jointly and severally repay the plaintiff a loan of 1,500 yuan in silver, plus interest at a rate of 1.5% per month from February 1st of this year until the end of execution, and jointly and severally repay the plaintiff a promissory note for 1,326 yuan in silver, plus interest at an annual rate of 5% from the due date until the end of execution; the remainder of the plaintiff's claim is rejected; litigation costs borne by Zhang Zhiming, Jiang Hengchang, and Pan Dasheng. ▲ Lü Hongda vs. Yang Fangxin for debt: Appeal dismissed; costs of the second instance (regarding the appeal) and the third instance before retrial are borne by the appellant.

▲ Criminal Judgments: Police Department vs. Yu Tangdi for gambling: Yu Tangdi, i.e., Katada, a habitual gambler, sentenced to eight months imprisonment and fined 400 yuan. ▲ Police Department vs. Wu Caiying et al. for opium: Wu Caiying and Zhang Zhusan, each convicted of one count of opium use, each sentenced to two months imprisonment, with a two-year suspended sentence. ▲ Police Department vs. Hou Gui, et al. for opium: Hou Gui sentenced to three months imprisonment for helping to provide premises for people to use opium; Zhen Jinlin and Lin Ting sentenced to one month imprisonment for opium use. ▲ Police Department vs. Wang Zhangshi et al. for opium: Wang Zhangshi sentenced to six months imprisonment for providing premises for people to use opium substitutes; Zhang Juren, Qiao Ayi, Li Arer, and Hu Bingsheng sentenced to one month imprisonment for opium substitute use; Zhang Huaren and Wu Bingsheng each given a two-year suspended sentence; Cai Sihai and Jin Yishi acquitted. ▲ Shen A'ming, a recidivist, sentenced to three months imprisonment for providing premises for people to use opium; Huang Yuexiang, San Shaoting, and Zhu Heshang sentenced to three months imprisonment each for opium use. ▲ Shen Shanyu sentenced to six months imprisonment and fined 300 yuan for providing premises for people to use opium; Hong Yongfu, Hong Zhixie, Mao Songren, and Lü Kehang sentenced to one month imprisonment each and fined 100 yuan for opium use; two-year suspended sentence for Hong Yongfu and Mao Songren. ▲ Two-year suspended sentence for Yang Zhiren; Li Chunhua sentenced to three months imprisonment for helping to provide premises for people to use opium; Luo Zhanglin, Wang Bingqing, and Zhang Ziyun sentenced to one month imprisonment each for opium use; two-year suspended sentence for Zhang Ziyun. ▲ Hou Huogen sentenced to six months imprisonment for providing premises for people to use opium; Cao Haiwang, Zhao Bing, and Fei Yuanxiang sentenced to one month imprisonment each for opium use; two-year suspended sentence for Zhao Abing and Fei Yuanxiang. ▲ Police Department vs. Qi Hezhang for assault: Qi Hezhang fined 20 yuan for physical assault. ▲ Police Department vs. Guo Mingting et al. for obstructing public duty: Guo Mingting and Luo Zhao sentenced to four months imprisonment each for jointly using violence and coercion against public officials lawfully performing their duties; each given a two-year suspended sentence; acquitted on the remaining charge of document forgery. ▲ Police Department vs. Shen Jushan for theft: Shen Jushan, a recidivist thief, sentenced to four months imprisonment. Shanghai Local Court 236

▲ Civil Judgments: Shi Quangui vs. Xu Hongbing for mortgage: The ships sold by the plaintiff should be used to offset the defendant's debt by 350 (units); the defendant should repay the plaintiff 436 yuan in silver in monthly installments as agreed; Ship No. 18048 owned by the defendant should be temporarily held in the plaintiff's custody; provisional execution of the third item listed above should be announced; the remainder of the plaintiff's claim is rejected; the defendant's partial counterclaim is rejected; litigation costs borne by the plaintiff, counterclaim costs borne equally by both parties. ▲ Lin Jusheng vs. Wang Zhisheng for loan: The defendant should repay the plaintiff a loan of 200 yuan in silver, plus interest calculated at a rate of 1.5% per month from February 1, 1932 until the end of execution. ▲ Fan Xiaorui vs. Le Ayou for loan: The defendant should repay the plaintiff 500 yuan in silver; litigation costs, excluding one-sixth of the withdrawn portion borne by the plaintiff, the remainder borne by the defendant Dai Weian by one-sixth, and Cheng Zhangshi and Wang Jinzhang by two-sixths each. ▲ Xu Fuquan vs. He Yutian for goods payment: The defendant should repay the plaintiff 110 yuan in silver for goods; litigation costs borne by the plaintiff. Zhang Biao vs. Sun Baji et al. for rice payment: Defendant Sun Baji should repay the plaintiff 390 yuan in silver for rice; defendant Su Yougui should repay the plaintiff 140 yuan in silver for rice; defendant Wang Hedian should repay the plaintiff 290 yuan in silver for rice; defendant Ruichang Hao should repay the plaintiff 270 yuan in silver for rice; Tang Yueming should repay the plaintiff 180 yuan in silver for rice; He Xing should repay the plaintiff 290 yuan in silver for rice; Xie Xing Company should repay the plaintiff 85 yuan in silver for rice; litigation costs to be borne by the defendants proportionally. ▲ Zhang Changyou et al. vs. Jiang Chunfang for appeal against eviction: Appeal dismissed; costs of the second instance to be borne by the appellants proportionally. ▲ Ji Company vs. Huang Zhiqing should repay the plaintiff mortgage silver 18,500 taels, including 11,000 taels of silver from August 30, 1930, 4,000 taels of silver from December 7, 1930, and 3,500 taels of silver from February 15, 1931, until the end of execution, and should pay the agreed interest calculated at 1.2% per month; if Huang Zhiqing is unable to repay, defendants Zhu Ruisheng and Chen Shaoqin should jointly bear the responsibility for repayment on his behalf; litigation costs, excluding one-fourth of the withdrawn portion borne by the plaintiff, the remaining three-fourths borne by defendant Huang Zhiqing but. ▲ Shen Lingen vs. Wang Bingsheng for appeal against tenant relocation loan: In addition to rejecting the loan portion, the original judgment is changed; the respondent should pay the appellant 15 yuan in silver for rent and transfer the five-fen field located at Map 1, Section 20, Nanhui County, to the appellant for management; the remainder of the appellant's claims in the first instance and the remainder of the appeal are rejected; three-fourths of the first and second instance litigation costs borne by the respondent, one-fourth borne by the appellant.

▲ Criminal Judgments: Chen Zhaolang and Jin Xianying each sentenced to six months imprisonment for helping Tang Xiaogen obtain illegal profits through fraudulent means. ▲ Sun Renbiao's lawsuit against Qiang Renyao for assault: This private prosecution is not accepted. ▲ Xu Zhicheng's lawsuit against Shao Amao et al. for obstructing freedom: This private prosecution is not accepted. ▲ Ruling: Yuan Qifa's false accusation and opium case: Yuan Qifa's trial suspended. ▲ Wang Changlin's opium case: Sentenced to six months imprisonment and fined 300 yuan for possession of opium with intent to sell. ▲ Chen Fengxian's embezzlement case: Chen Fengxian sentenced to three months imprisonment for embezzling items held in the course of business. ▲ Ruling: Zhu Canyun et al.'s intimidation case: Zhu Canyun and Xin Fayou's trials suspended. ▲ The magistrate of Chuansha County's case regarding Hu Jixi et al.'s suspected theft and fraud: This case should be transferred to the jurisdiction of the Baoshan County government. ▲ Jiang Xuping's lawsuit against Cao Siyin for breach of trust: This private prosecution is dismissed. ▲ Yu Xiangfa's lawsuit against Wang Fuqing for embezzlement and breach of trust: This private prosecution is dismissed. ▲ Qian Yuezhu's lawsuit against Chen Zhixin for abandonment: This private prosecution is dismissed. ▲ The prosecutor of this court's appeal case regarding Ni Shuiru et al.'s opium use: The original judgment is reversed; Ni Shuiru sentenced to three months imprisonment and fined 30 yuan for opium use; Ni Wushi sentenced to two months imprisonment and fined 20 yuan for attempted opium use; each given a three-year suspended sentence. ▲ Li Qingfeng sentenced to one year and six months imprisonment for colluding with three or more people to snatch other people's property. ▲ Zhang Caiji et al.'s obstruction of family case: Zhang Caiji sentenced to one year imprisonment for each of four counts of receiving abducted men and women under the age of twenty with intent to profit; determined execution term of one year and six months. ▲ Lin Caihua's trial suspended. ▲ Wang Dadan sentenced to one month imprisonment and fined 30 yuan for opium use. ▲ Wang Fengshi et al.'s opium case: Wang Fengshi, Chen Zenger, and Miao Zhusan sentenced to one month imprisonment each and fined 30 yuan for opium use. ▲ Du Caiyuan's obstruction of family case: Du Caiyuan sentenced to six months imprisonment for enticing a woman under the age of twenty to leave her person with parental authority with intent to commit adultery. ▲ Cai Rongtang, i.e., Sun Rongtang, sentenced to one year imprisonment for intending to profit by selling opium. ▲ Zhang Youmei sentenced to imprisonment for robbery at the pier (Above dated July 30th)
